       iminā vijanidānena cittassa paṇidhihi ca  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ vinipātaṃ na gacchati 
  
       āraddhaviriyo pahitatto cetoguṇasamāhito  
 jātiyā pattavassohaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ  
  
       saṭṭhakappasahassambhi vijamānasanāmakā   
 soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vidhupanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  vidhupanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    sannidhāpaka  se    bijanikā  machasaṃ    santhā lokagganāyako  machasaṃ 
    vijanāmasamānakā  se bijamānasanāmakā  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
     sataraṃsikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       ucciyaṃ  selamāruya nisīdi purisuttamo  
 pabbatassāvidurambhi brāhmaṇo mantapāragu  
  
       upaviṭṭhaṃ mahāvīraṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 añajalimpaggahetvāna satthaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       esa buddho mahāvīro varadhammappakāsako  
 jalani aggikhandhova bhikkhusaṃghapurakkhato  
  
       mahāsamuddo vakkhobho aṇṇavova duruttaro  
 migarājāvasambhito dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā 
  
       mama saṅkappamaññāya padumuttaranāyako  
 bhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha  
  
       yenāyaṃ añajali dinno buddhāseṭṭho ca thomitato  
 tiṃsakappasahassāni devarajjaṃ karissati  
  
       kappasatasahassambhi aṃgirasasanāmako  
 vivattacchaddo  sambuddho uppajjissati tāvade  
  
       tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmito    
 sataraṃsiti nāmena arahā so bhavissati 
  
       jātiyā sattavassohaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
 sataraṃsimbhi nāmena pabhā niddhāvate mama  
  
       maṇḍape rukkhamule vā jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane  
  
       saṭṭhikappasahassambhi caturo rāma  nāmakā  
 sattaratanasampannā vakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sataraṃsiyo  thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sataraṃsikattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     sayanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa sabbalokānukampino  
 sayanaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ vippasannena cetasā  
  
       tena sayanadānena sukhette bijasampadā  
 bhogā nibbattare  tassa sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
    ubbiddhaṃ  machasaṃ    vicittachando  machasaṃ  se    roma     se    sataraṃsi  machasaṃ    bhogo nibbattate     se  
  
               
  
       ākāse seyyaṃ kappemi dharemi imaṃ  
 pāṇesu me issariyaṃ sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       pañcakappasahassambhi aṭṭha āsuṃ mahāvarā    
 catuttiṃse kappasate caturo ca mahabbalā  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sayanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sayanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     gandhodakiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa mahābodhimaho ahu  
 vicittaṃ ghaṭamādāya gandhodakamadāsahaṃ  
  
       nahāpanakāle bodhiyā  mahāmegho pavassatha  
 ninnādo ca mahā āsi  asaniyā phalantiyā  
  
       tenevāsanivegena tathe kālakato ahuṃ    
 devaloke ṭhito santo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsahaṃ  
  
              
  
       aho buddho aho dhammā aho no satthusampadā 
 kalebaraṃ me patitaṃ devaloke ramāmahaṃ 
  
       ubbadidhaṃ bhagavaṃ mayhaṃ satabhumaṃ samuggataṃ  
 kaññāsatasassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā  
  
       ābādhā me na vijjanti soko mayhaṃ na pijjati  
 pariḷāhaṃ na passāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
       aṭṭhavise kappasate rājā saṃvasito ahuṃ  
 sattaratanampanno cakakvatti mahabbalo  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhodakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  gandhodakiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     opavayha  ttherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa ājāniyamadāsahaṃ  
 niyyādetvāna sambuddhe  agamāsiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ  
  
       devalo nāma nāmena satthuno aggasāvako  
 varadhammassa dāyādo āgacchi mama santikaṃ  
  
    mahātejā  machasaṃ mahāvīrā  syā       nahānakāle ca bodhiyā  simu    ahuṃ        ahaṃ  machasaṃ    opavuyha  bahūsu    sambuddhaṃ     
  
               
  
       sapattahāro bhagavā ājāneyyo na kappati  
 tava saṅkappamaññāya adhivāsesi cakkhumā 
  
       agaghāpevo vātajavaṃ sindhavaṃ sighavāhanaṃ  
 padumuttarabuddhassa khamaniyamadāsahaṃ  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ   
 khamaniyā vātajavā  cittā  nibbattare  mama  
  
              
  
       lābhā tesaṃ suladdhaṃva ye labhantupasampadaṃ  
 punapi payirupāseyyaṃ buddho loke save bhave  
  
       aṭṭhavisatikkhattuṃhaṃ rājā āsiṃ mahabbalo  
 cāturanno vijitāvi jambusaṇḍassa  issaro  
  
       idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo  
 pattosmi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā opavayho thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  opavayhattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     saparicārāsanattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa piṇḍapātaṃ adāsahaṃ  
 gantvā taṃ bhojanaṭṭhānaṃ  mallikāhi parikkhipaṃ  
  
       tamhāsanambhi āsino buddho lokagganāyako  
 akittayi piṇḍapātaṃ ujubhuto samābito  
  
       yathāpi bhaddake khette bijaṃ appampi ropitaṃ  
 sammā dhāraṃ pavecchante phalaṃ toseti kassakaṃ  
  
       tathevāyaṃ piṇḍapāto sukhette ropito tayā  
 bave nibbattamāna ṃhi  phalato tosayissati  
  
       idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho jalajuttaranāmako  
 piṇḍapātaṃ thavitvāna   pakkāmi uttarāmukho  
  
    deve ca mānuse bhave  simu bhavane sabbadā mama        khamaniyaṃ vātajavaṃ  machasaṃ khamaniyo vātajavo  se ājāniyāvātajavā  syā    citte     se cittaṃ  machasaṃ    nibbattate  machasaṃ se    jambudipassa  syā    kiliṭṭhakaṭṭhānaṃ  machasaṃ se    parikkhittaṃ  machasaṃ    se    nibbattamānambhi  machasaṃ       phalante kappayissati  machasaṃ     gahetvāna  machasaṃ se  
  
               
  
       saṃvuto pātimokkhasmiṃ indriyesu ca pañcasu  
 pavicekamanuyutto viharāmi anāsavo  
  
              
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saparivārāsano thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  saparivārāsanattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     pañcadipakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa sabbabhūtānukampino  
 susaṇṭhahitvā  saddamme ujudiṭṭhi ahosahaṃ  
  
       padipadānaṃ pādāsiṃ parivāretvāna bodhiyaṃ  
 saddahanto padipāni akariṃ tāvade ahaṃ  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 kākāse ukkaṃ dhārenti dipādānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tirokuḍḍaṃ tiroselaṃ samatiggayha pabbataṃ  
 samantā yojanasataṃ dassanaṃ anubhomahaṃ  
  
       catuttiṃse kappasate satacakkhusanāmakā  
 rājāhesuṃ mahātejā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       tena kammāvasesena pattombhi āsavakkhayaṃ  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ dipadindassa sāsane  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcadipako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pañcadipaka ttherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     dhajadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa bodhimha pādaputtame  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena dhajamāropayiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       patita  pattāni gaṇhitvā bahiddhā chaḍḍhayiṃ ahaṃ  
 antosuddhaṃ bahisuddhaṃ adhimuttamanāsavaṃ  
 sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ acandiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ  
  
              
  
       padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho  
 bhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha  
  
    saddahitvāna  machasaṃ se    satta  se a pana      padipadāyaka  
  
               
  
       iminā dhajadānena upaṭṭhānena cubhayaṃ  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggahassaṃ duggatiṃ so na gacchati  
  
       devesu devasobhaggaṃ  anubhossatanappakaṃ  
 anekasatakkhattuñca rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati  
 uggato nāma nāmena cakkamatti bhavissati  
  
       sampattiṃ anubhotvāna sukkamūlena codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato sāsanebhiramissati  
  
       padhānapabhitattombhi upasanto nirūpadhi  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane  
  
       ekapaññāsasahasse kappe uggatasavahayo  
 paññāsatisahasse  khattiyo meghasamahayo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhajadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  dhajadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     padumattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       catusaccaṃ pakāsento varadhammappavattako   
 vassate amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ nibbāpento mahājanaṃ  
  
       sadaṇḍaṃ  padumaṃ gayha aḍḍhakose ṭhito ahaṃ  
 padumuttaramunissa haṭṭho ukkhipimambare  
  
       āgacchante ca padume ababhuto āsi tāvado  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya paggaṇhi vadataṃ varo  
  
       karaseṭṭhena paggayha jalajaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ  
 bhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha  
  
       yenidaṃ padumaṃ khittaṃ sabbaññumbhi vināyake    
 tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato  
  
              
  
       tiṃsa kappāni devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  
 pathavyā rajjaṃ sattasataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati  
  
       tattha pattaṃ gaṇetvāna  cakkavatti bhavissati  
 ākāsato pupphavuṭṭhi abhivassissati tadā  
  
       kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati  
  
    sobhāgyaṃ     se    paññāsasatasahasse  machasaṃ    se    caradhammacakkappavattako        sadhajaṃ     se a    sabbaññutamanāyake  syā    se    gahetvāna  simu 
  
               
  
       tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
       nikkhamitvāna kucchimhā sampajāno patissato  
 jātiyā pañcavassohaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  padumattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     asanabodhiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       jātiyā sattavassohaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ  
  
       tissassāhaṃ bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena ropayiṃ bodhimuttaṃ  
  
       asano nāmadheyyena dharaṇi rūhapādapo  
 pañca vasse paricariṃ asanaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ  
  
       pupphitaṃ pādapaṃ dismā abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ  
 sakaṃ kammaṃ pakittento buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upāgamiṃ  
  
       tisso tadā so sambuddho sayambhu aggapuggalo  
 bhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha  
  
       yenāyaṃ ropitā bodhi buddhapujā ca sakkatā  
 tamahaṃ kittayissami suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
              
  
       tiṃsa kappāni devesu devarajjaṃ karissati  
 catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ so cakkavatti bhavissati  
  
       tusātā biba cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito  
 dve sampatti anubhotvā manussatte ramissati  
  
       padhānapabhitatto so upasanto nirūpadhi  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
               
  
       vivekamanuyuttohaṃ upasanto nirūpadhi  
 nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe bodhiṃ ropesahaṃ tadā 
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhiropassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catusattatito kappe daṇḍasenoti vissuto  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti tadā ahuṃ  
  
       tesattatimbhito kappe sattāhesuṃ mahīpati  
 samattanemi nāmena rājāto cakkamattino 
  
       paṇṇavisatito kappe puṇṇako nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā asanabodhiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  asanabodhiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 vijani sataraṃsi ca sayanodaki vāhiyo 
 parivāro padipañca dhajo padumapujako 
 bodhi ca dasamo vutto gāthā dve navuti tathā  
  vijanivaggo jaṭṭho  
  
     sakacintaniya  ttherāpadānaṃ 
  
       pavanaṃ kānanaṃ disvā appasadadamanāvilaṃ  
 isinaṃ anuciṇṇaṃva āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
  
       thupaṃ katvāna pulinaṃ  nānāpupphaṃ samokiriṃ  
 sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ nimmitaṃ abhivandahaṃ  
  
              
  
       satatratanasampanenā rājā raṭṭhambhi  issaro  
 sakakammābhiraddhohaṃ thupapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekatavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thuppujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       asitikappenattayaso cakkavatti ahosahaṃ  
 sattaratanasampanno catudipambhi issaro  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sakavittaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sakavittanisattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    sakavintiya  sīmu    veḷunā    se a    raṭṭhasami  machasaṃ si mu 
  
               
  
     avopupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vihārā abhinikkhamma abbhuṭṭhabhiya  caṅkame  
 catusaccaṃ pakāsento deseti  deseti  amataṃ padaṃ  
  
       sikhissa giramaññāya buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino  
 nānāpupphaṃ gahetvāna ākāsambhi samokiriṃ  
  
       tena kammena dipadinde lokajeṭṭhe narāsabho  
 pattombhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito visatikappambhi sumedho nāma khattiyo  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā avo pupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  avopupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
              
  
     paccāgamaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       sindhuyā nadiyā tīre cakkavāko ahaṃ tadā  
 suddhasevālabhakkhohaṃ pāpesu ca susaññato  
  
       addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ gacchantaṃ anilañajase  
 tuṇḍena sālaṃ  paggayha vipassissā bhiropayiṃ  
  
       yassa saddhā tathāgate acalā suppatiṭṭhitā  
 tena cittappasādena duggatiṃ so na gacchati 
  
       svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 vihaṅgamena santena subijaṃ ropitaṃ mayā  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
       sucārudassanā nāma aṭṭheta ekanāmakā  
 kappe sattarase āsu cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paccagamaniyo  thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  paccāgamaniyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
    abbhuṭṭhāsi     a abbhuṭṭhāhi ca se    desetto    se a    dipadinda  lokajeṭṭha  narāsabha   iti sabbattha     āvo     se    mālaṃ  se    saddhāgamaniya se 
  
               
  
     parappasādakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       usahaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ mahesiṃ vijitāvinaṃ  
 suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ ko disvā nappasidati  
  
       himavā vāparimeyyo sāgarova duruttaro  
 tatheva jhānaṃ buddhassa  ko disvā nappasiditi  
  
       vasudhā yathā appameyyā cittā vanavaṭaṃsakā  
 tatheva sīlaṃ buddhassa ko disvā nappasiditi  
  
       anilajova asaṅkhobhā  yathākāso asaṅkhiyo  
 tatheva ñāṇaṃ buddhassa ko disvā nappasiditi  
  
              
  
       imāhi catugāthāhi  brāhmaṇo senasamhayo  
 buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thavitvāna siddhatthaṃ aparājitaṃ  
  
       catunavutikappāni duggatiṃ nupapajjatha    
 sugatisu susampattiṃ  anubhosi  anappakaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe thavitvā lokanāyakaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thomanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catuddasambhi kappambi caturo āsumuggatā  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā parappasādako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  parappasādakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     bhisadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       vessabhu nāma nāmena isinaṃ tatiyo ahu  
 kānanaṃ vanamogayha vihāsi purisuttamo  
  
       bhisaṃ mulālaṃ gaṇhitvā agamaṃ  buddhasantikaṃ  
 taṃ ca buddhassa pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       karena ca parāmaṭṭho vessabhuvarabudadhinā  
 sukhāhaṃ nābhijānāmi samaṃ tena tatuttariṃ  
  
       carimo vattate mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā  
 hatthināgena santena kusalaṃ ropitaṃ mayā  
  
    devadevassa  se    anilañajasāsaṃkhubbho        catūhi gāthāhi     se    nupapajjahaṃ     se    sugatiṃ sukhasampattiṃ  machasaṃ    anubhomi  se anubhosiṃ        āsuṃ uggatā  se       āgamma  se 
  
               
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       samodhānā ca rājāno soḷasa manujādhipā  
 kappambhi terase āsuṃ cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhisadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  bhisadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
              
  
     sucintitattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       giriduggacaro āsiṃ abhijātova kesarī  
 migasaṃghaṃ vadhitvāna jivāmi pabbatantare  
  
       atthadassi tu bhagavā sabbaññu vadataṃ varo  
 mamuddharitukāmo so āgacchi pabbatuttamaṃ  
  
       pasadañca migaṃ hanatvā bhakkhituṃ samupāgamiṃ  
 bhagavā tambhi samaye bhikkhamāno  upāgami  
  
       varamaṃsāni paggayha adāsiṃ tassa satthuno  
 anumodi mahāvīro nibbāpento mamaṃ tadā  
  
       tena cittappasādena giriduggaṃ pavisahaṃ  
 pitiṃ uppādayitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
       etena maṃsadānena cittassa paṇidhihi ca  
 paṇṇarase kappasate devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       avasesesu kappesu kusalaṃ nicitaṃ  mayā  
 teneva maṃsadānena buddhānussaraṇena ca  
  
       aṭṭhatiṃsambhi kappambhi aṭṭha dighāyutāmakā  
 saṭṭhimbhito kappasate duve varūṇanāmakā  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucintito thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sucittitattherassa apadānaṃ jaṭṭhaṃ   
  
    bhikkhayāno se    kāritaṃ se    cintataṃ  machasaṃ karitaṃ  syā 
  
               
              
  
     vatthadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       pakkhijāto tadā āsiṃ suvaṇṇo garūḷādhipo  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ gacchantaṃ gandhamādanaṃ  
  
       jabhitvā garuḷaṃ  vaṇṇaṃ māṇavakaṃ adhārayiṃ  
 ekaṃ vatthaṃ mayā dinnaṃ dipadindassa tādino  
  
       tañca dussaṃ paṭiggayha buddho lokagganāyako  
 antaḷikkhe ṭhito satthā imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha  
  
       iminā vatthadānena cittassa paṇidhibhi ca  
 pahāya garuḷaṃ yoniṃ devaloke ramissati 
  
       atthadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 vatthadānaṃ pasaṃsitvā pakkāmi uttarāmukho  
  
       bhave tibbattamānambhi honti me vatthasampadā  
 ākase chadanaṃ hoti vatthadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       aruṇakā  satta janā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
 chattiṃsatimbhi kappambhi āsiṃsu manujādhipā  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā catthadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  catthadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     ambadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       anomadassi bhagavā nisinno pabbatantare  
 mettāya aphari lokaṃ appamāṇaṃ nirūpadhi  
  
       kapi ahaṃ tadā āsiṃ bhimavante taguttame  
 disvā anomaṃ amitaṃ buddhe cittaṃ padādayiṃ  
  
       himavatantassa avidūre  ambāsuṃ phalino tadā  
 tato pakkaṃ gahetvāna ambaṃ samadhukaṃ adaṃ  
  
              
  
       tamme buddho viyākāsi anomadassi mahāmuni  
 iminā madhudānena ambadānena cubhayaṃ  
  
       sattapaññāsa kappāni devaloke ramissati  
 avasesesu kappesu vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsarissati  
  
       khepetvā pāpakaṃ kammaṃ paripakkāya buddhiyā  
 vinipātamagantvāna  kilese jhāpayissati 
  
       damena uttamenāhaṃ damitomabi mahesinā  
 pattombhi acalaṃ  ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
    garuḷā  machasaṃ       aruṇavā  machasaṃ    avidūre himavantassa  sabbattha     vinipātādiyāgantvā     se    amataṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       sattasattatikappasate ambaṭṭhaja sanāmakā  
 catuddasā te rājāno cakkavatati mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ambadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     sumanattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       sumano nāma nāmena mālākāro ahaṃ tadā 
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ  
  
       ubho hatthehi paggayha sumanaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ  
 buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sikhino lokabandhuno  
  
       imāya pupphapujāya cetanāpaṇidhibhi ca  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       chabbisatimbhi kappambhi cattārosuṃ  mahāyasā  
 sattarananasampanno rājāno cakkavattino  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumano thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sumanattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
              
  
     pupphacaṅgoṭiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       abhitarūpaṃ sihaṃva abhijātaṃva kesariṃ  
 vyagghusabhaṃva pavaraṃ garūḷaggaṃva pakkhinaṃ    
  
       sikhiṃ tilokasaraṇaṃ anejaṃ aparājitaṃ  
 nisinnaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ bhikkhusaṃghapurakkhataṃ  
  
       vaṅgoṭake ṭhapetvāna anojaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ  
 saha caṅgoṭakoneva buddhaseṭṭhaṃ samākiraṃ  
  
       tena cittappasādena dipadinde narāsabhe  
 pattombhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sampuṇṇe tiṃsakappambhi devabhūtisanāmakā  
 sattarananasampanno pañcasuṃ cakkavattino  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphacaṅgoṭiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pupphacaṅgoṭiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
    āyutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ    se    cattārassu     se  atita rūpaṃ sihaṃca garuḷaggaṃva pakkhinaṃ  iti mudditapotthakesu dissate    dipadinda narāsabha   sabbattha  
  
               
  
 uddānaṃ  
 sakacinti avopupphi paccābhigamanena ca 
 parappasādi bhisado sucinti vatthadāyako 
 ambadāyī ca sumano pupphacaṅgoṭiyopi ca 
 gāthekasattati vuttā gaṇitā atthadassi bhi  
  sakavittaniyavaggo sattamo   
  
              
  
     nāgasamāgattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       āpāṭaliṃ  ahaṃ pupphaṃ uccitasmiṃ mahāpathe    
 phupambhi abhiropesiṃ sikhino lokabandhuno  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thupapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito paṇṇarase kappe bhumiyo nāma khattiyo  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nāgasamalo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  nāgasamālattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ    
  
     padasaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       akkantaṃ ca padaṃ disvā tissassādiccabandhuno  
 heṭṭhā haṭṭhena cittena pāde cittaṃ pasādayi  
  
       devanavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi padasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito sattamake kappe sumedho nāma khattiyo  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
      paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  padasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
    apāṭaliṃ  sabbattha    ujjhitaṃ sumahāpathe  sabbattha  theragāthaṭṭhakathāyaṃ panassa therassa visadisaṃ apadānaṃ dissati  
  
               
              
  
     buddhasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       dumagge paṃsukūlikaṃ laggaṃ disvāna satthuno  
 tato tamañajaliṃ katvā paṃsukūlaṃ avandahaṃ  
  
       dve navute ito kappe yaṃ kammakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito catutthake kappe dumasārosi khattiyo   
 cāturanto vijitāvi cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  buddhasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     bhisāluvadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       kānanaṃ vanamogayha vasāmi vipine  ahaṃ  
 vipassiṃ addasaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
  
       bhisāluvañca pādāsiṃ udakaṃ hatthadhovanaṃ  
 canditvā sirasā pāde pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho  
  
       ekatavute ito kappe bhisāluvamadaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi puññākammassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito tatiyo kappe bhisasammatakhattiyo  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhisāluvadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  bhisāluvadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
              
  
     ekasaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       khaṇḍo nāmāsi nāmena vipassissaggasāvako  
 ekā bhikkhā mayā dinnā lokāhutipaṭiggahe  
  
       tena cittappasādena dipadinde narāsabhe    
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ekabhikkhāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    saññakattherāpadānaṃ  se    a    dumasāro sukhattiyo    se    vi cane  a       dipadinda narāsabha  simu machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       cattāḷise ito kappe varuṇo nāma khattiyo  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ekasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     tiṇasantharadāyakattherāpadānaṃ       bhimavantassa avidūre mahājātassaro ahu  
 satapattehi sañachanno nānāsakuṇamālayo  
  
       tambhi nahātvā pitvā ca avidūre vasāmahaṃ  
 addasaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ gacchantaṃ anilañajaye  
  
       mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke anuttaro  
 vyambhato orubhitvāna bhumiyaṭṭhāsi tāvade  
  
       visāṇena tiṇaṃ gayha nisidanamadāsahaṃ  
 nisīdi bhagavā tisso lokegganāyako  
  
       sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā avandiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 patikuṭiko  apasakkiṃ  nijjhāyanto mahāmuniṃ  
  
       tena cittappasādena nimmāṇaṃ uppajjahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi santharassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       ito dutiyeke kappe migasammatakhattiyo  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇasattharadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tiṇasantharadākattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     sucidāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       tiṃsakappasahassambhi sambuddho lokenayako  
 sumedho nāma nāmena khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo  
  
       tassa kañcanavaṇṇassa dipadindassa tādino  
 pañca suci mayā dinnā sibbanatthāya cīvaraṃ  
  
    lokavināyako        paṭikuṭiko  machasaṃ ukkuṭiko  syā paṭikkuṭiko  se 
    avasakkiṃ  se    
  
               
  
       teneva sucidānena nipuṇatthavipassakaṃ  
 tikkhaṃ lahuñca phāsuñca ñāṇaṃ me udapajjatha  
  
       dipadādhipati nāma rājāno caturo ahuṃ  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sucidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     pāṭalipupaphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       seṭṭhiputto tadā āsiṃ sukhumālo sukhedhito 
 ucchaṅge pāṭalipupphaṃ katvā taṃ abhisaṃhariṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe  
 kañcanagghiyasaṅkāsaṃ dvatatiṃsa  varalakkhaṇaṃ  
  
              
  
       haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena pupphena  abhipujayīṃ  
 tissaṃ lokaviduṃ nāthaṃ naradevaṃ namassahaṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito tesaṭṭhikappambhi abhisammatanāmako  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāṭalipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pāṭalaṭipupaphiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     ṭhitañajaliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ  
 tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ tissaṃ pavaralakkhaṇaṃ  
  
       tassāhaṃ  añjaliṃ katvā pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho  
 avidūre nisinnassa niyake paṇṇasatthare  
  
       tato me asanipāto matthake nipati tadā  
 sohaṃ maraṇakālambhi akāsiṃ punarañajaliṃ  
  
    khattiṃsa  machasaṃ    pupphehi machasaṃ se    tatthāhaṃ  machasaṃ     ayaṃ gāthā asamiṃ apadāne paṭhamagāthāvasne potthakesu dissate  
  
               
  
       dvenavute ito kappe añjaliṃ akariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi añajalissa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catupaññāsakappambhi migaketu sanāmako  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ṭhitañajaliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ṭhitañajaliyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
              
  
     tipadumiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu  
 danto dantaparivuto nagarā nikkhami jino  
  
       nagare haṃsavatiyā ahosiṃ māliko tadā  
 yaṃ tattha uttamaṃ pupphaṃ tīṇi pupphāni  aggahiṃ  
  
       addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ paṭimaggantarāpaṇe  
 sohaṃ  disvāna sambuddhaṃ evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā  
  
       kimme imehi pupphehi rañño upanatehi  me  
 gāmaṃ vā gāmakkhettaṃ vā sahassaṃ vā labheyyahaṃ  
  
       adantadamakaṃ dhiraṃ sabbasattasukhāvahaṃ  
 lokanāthaṃ pujayitvā lacchāmi amataṃ dhanaṃ 
  
       evāhaṃ cintayitvāna sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 tīṇilohitake gayha ākāse ukkhipiṃ  tadā  
  
       mayā ukkhittamattambhi ākāse patthariṃsu  te  
 dhāriṃsu matthake tattha uddhaṃvaṇṭā adhomukhā  
  
       ye keci manujā disvā ukkuṭṭhiṃ sampavattayuṃ  
 devatā antaḷikkhamhi sādhukāraṃ pavattayuṃ  
  
    padamapupphā  machasaṃ    sabha  se    upanitehi  sabbattha    ukakiraṃ  se    ukakiraṃsu se 
  
               
  
       accheraṃ loke uppannaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā  
 sabbe dhammaṃ suṇissāma pupphānaṃ cāhasā mayaṃ 
  
       padumutataro lokavidu āhuninaṃ paṭiggaho  
 vithiyaṃ hi ṭhito satthā  imā gāthā abhāsatha  
  
       yo so buddhaṃ apūjesi rattapadmebhi  māṇavo  
 tamhaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato  
  
       tiṃsa kappasahassāni devaloke ramissati  
 tiṃsa kappāni devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  
  
       mahācitthārikaṃ nāmaṃ vyamhaṃ hessati tāvade  
 tiyojanasatubbedhaṃ diyaḍḍhasatavitthataṃ  
  
              
  
       cattāri satasahassāni niyyuhā ca sumāpitā  
 kūṭāgāravarūpetā mahāsayanavositā  
  
       koṭisatasahassāyo parivāressanti accharā 
 kusalā naccagitassa vādinepi padakkhiṇā 
  
       etādise vyamhavare nārigaṇasamākule  
 vassissati pupphavasso dibbo lohitako sadā  
  
       bhittikhile nāgadante dvārabāhāya  toraṇe  
 cakkamattā lobhitakā olambissanti tāvade  
  
       patetana pattasañachanne  antovyamhavare idha  
 attharitvā pārupitvā tuvaṭṭissanti tāvade  
  
       bhavanaṃ parivāretvā samantā satayojanaṃ  
 te visuddhā lohitakā dibbagandhaṃ pavāyare  
  
       pañcasattatikkhattuññaca cakkavatti bhavissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ  
  
       sampattiyo duve bhutvā aniti anupadadavo  
 sampatte pariyosāne nibbāṇaṃ phassayissati 
  
       sudiṭṭho vata me buddho vāṇijjaṃ suppayojitaṃ  
 padamāni  tīṇi pujetvā anubhosiṃ tisampadaṃ  
  
       ajja me dhammappattassa vippamuttassa sabbaso  
 supupphitaṃ lohitakaṃ dhārayissati matthake  
  
    santo  se    rattapadumbhi  sīmu    dvārabābhe  se    pattaṃ piñajarena  se    padumāni  se    
  
               
  
       mama kammaṃ  kathentassa padumuttarasatthuno  
 sattapāṇasahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu  
  
       sattasahasse ito kappe yaṃ buddhamebhabipujayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tiṇṇaṃ padumānidaṃ  phalaṃ  
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā  
 sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tipadumiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tipadumiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 nāgasamālo padasaññi sasaññoluvadāyako 
 ekasaññi tiṇadado suci pāṭalipupphiyo 
 ṭhitañajali tipadumi gāthāyo pañcasattati  
  nāgasamālavaggo aṭṭhamo  
  
     timirapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       candabhāgānaditire anusotaṃ vajāmahaṃ  
 nisinnaṃ samaṇaṃ disvā vippasannamanāvilaṃ  
  
       tattha  cittaṃ pasādetvā evaṃ cinetasahaṃ tadā  
 tārayissati tiṇṇoyaṃ dantoyaṃ damayissati  
  
       assāsessati asasattho santo ca samayissati  
 mocayissati mutto ca nibbāpessati nibbuto 
  
       evaṃ saṃ  cintayitvāna siddhattassa mahesino  
 gahetvā timiraṃ pupphaṃ matthake okiriṃ ahaṃ  
  
       añjaliṃ paggahetvāna katvāna ca padakkhīṇaṃ  
 canditvā satthuno pāde pakkāmiṃ aparaṃ disaṃ  
  
    dhammaṃ  se    tīṇipadumātidaṃ   sabbattha     tassa  se       evāhaṃ  sabbattha  
  
               
  
       aciraṃ gatamatataṃ maṃ migarājā viheṭhayi   
 papānamanugacchanto tattheva papatiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyadaṃ phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       chapaññāsambhi kappambhi sattevāsuṃ mahāyasā  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā timirapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tipadumiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     gatasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       jātiyā sattavassohaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
 avandiṃ satthuno pāde vippasannena cetasā  
  
       satta naṅgalikipupphe ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ  
 tissaṃ buddhaṃ samuddissa anantaguṇasāgaraṃ  
  
       sugatānugataṃ  maggaṃ pujetvā haṭṭhamānaso 
 añajaliñca tadākāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakari tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito aṭṭhamake kappe tayo aggisibā ahuṃ  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gatasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  gatasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
              
  
     nipannañajaliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       rukkhamule nisinnohaṃ vyādhito paramena ca  
 paramakāruññapattombhi araññe kānate ahaṃ  
  
       anukampaṃ upādāyaṃ tisso satthā upesi maṃ  
 sohaṃ nipannako sanetā sire katvāna añjaliṃ  
  
    apilayī  machasaṃ se    sugatena gataṃ  aṭṭhakathā  
  
               
  
       pasanānacitto sumano sabbasattānamuttemaṃ  
 sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā tattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ vandaṃ purisuttamaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito pañcamake kappe pañcevāsuṃ mahāsikhā  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nipantañaliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  nipantajaliyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     adhopupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       abhibhu nāma so bhikkhu sikhino aggasāvako  
 mahānubhāvo tevijjo himavannaṃ upāgami  
  
       ahampi himavantambhi ramaniyassame isi  
 vasāmi appamaññāsu iddhisu ca tadā vasi  
  
       pakkhajāto viyākāse pabbataṃ adhivattayiṃ   
 adhopupphaṃ gahetvāna āgacchiṃ  pabbataṃ ahaṃ  
  
       satta pupphāni gaṇahitvā matthake okiriṃ ahaṃ  
 ālokite ca cirena  pakakāmiṃ pācināmukho  
  
              
  
       āvāsaṃ abhisambhosiṃ patvāna assamaṃ ahaṃ  
 khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna pāvisiṃ  pabbatattaraṃ  
  
       ajagaro maṃ piḷesi ghorarūpo mahabbalo  
 pubbakammaṃ saritvāna kattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā adhopupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  adhopupaphiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
    tadāgami  se machasaṃ    abhipatheyiṃ  se    abhimatthayiṃ  machasaṃ    agacchiṃ  machasaṃ    dhine  se    pāyāsiṃ  se machasaṃ  
  
               
  
     raṃsisaññakattherāpādanaṃ 
  
       pabbate himavantambhi vāsaṃ kappesahaṃ pure  
 ajinuttaravāsohaṃ  vasāmi pabbatantare  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ sataraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ  
 vanantaragataṃ disvā sālarājaṃva pupphitaṃ  
  
       raṃsyā  cittaṃ pasādevo vipassissa mahesino  
 paggayha añjaliṃ vandiṃ sirasā ukkuṭi  ahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi raṃsisaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā raṃsisaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  raṃsiyaññakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcaṃ   
  
              
  
     dutiyaraṃsisaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       pabbate himavantambhi vākaciradharo ahaṃ  
 caṅkamañca samārūḷho nisīdiṃ pācināmukho  
  
       pabbate sugataṃ disvā phussaṃ jhānarataṃ tadā  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna raṃsyā  cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi raṃsisaññayidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā raṃsisaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  dutiyaraṃsisaññakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     phaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       pabbate himavantambhi khurājinadharo ayaṃ  
 phussaṃ jinavaraṃ disvā phalahattho phalaṃ adaṃ  
  
       yamahaṃ phalamadāsiṃ vippasannena cetasā  
 bhave nibbattamānambhi phalaṃ nibbattate mama  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ adadiṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā phaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  phaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
    ajinuttamavatthohaṃ        raṃse  machasaṃ    se    sirasukakuṭiko  machasaṃ    raṃse  sabbathe  
  
               
              
  
     saddasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       pabbate himavantambhi vasāmi paṇṇasatthare  
 phussassa dhammaṃ bhaṇato sadde cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakari tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saddasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  saddasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     bodhisiñcakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       vipassissa bhagavato mahābodhimaho ahu  
 pabbajjupagato santo upagacchiṃ mahaṃ ahaṃ  
  
       kusumodakamādāya bodhiyā okiriṃ ahaṃ  
 mocayissati no mutto nibbāpessati nibbuto 
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ bodhimabhisiñcayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhisiñcāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tettiṃse vattamānambhi kappe āsuṃ janādhipā  
 udakāsecanā nāma aṭṭhete cakkavattino  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhisiñcako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  bodhisiñcakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
              
  
     padumapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       pokkharavanaṃ paviṭṭho bhañajanto padumānahaṃ  
 addasaṃ phussasamabuddhaṃ khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ  
  
       padumapupphaṃ gahetvāna ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ  
 pasannakammaṃ katvāna  pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
  
       pabbajitvāna kayena manasā saṃvutena ca  
 vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ  
  
    mahā tadā     bodhisaññāyidaṃ       bodhisaññako      pāpakammaṃ karitvāna  a sīmu  
  
               
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayi  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       padumāhāsanāmā aṭṭhārasa mahipani  
 aṭṭhārassu kappesu aṭṭhatāḷisamāsisuṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumapupaphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  padumapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 timira naṅgalipupphi nipannañajaliko adho 
 dve raṃsisaññi phalado saddasaññi ca secako 
 padumapupphi ca gāthāyo chappaññāsa pakittitā  
  timirapupphiyavaggo navamo   
  
              
  
     sudhāpiṇḍiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       pujārahe pujayato buddhe yadi ca sāvake 
 papañcasamatikkante tiṇṇasokaparidadave  
  
       te tādise pujato nibbute akutobhaye  
 na sakkā puññaṃ saṅkhātuṃ idamettamapi  keneci  
  
       catunnamapi dipānaṃ issaraṃ yodha kāraye  
 ekissā pujanāyetaṃ kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasiṃ  
  
       siddhatthassa naraggassa cetiye eḷitantare  
 sudhāpiṇḍo mayā dinno vippasannena cetasā  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakari tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi paṭisaṅkhārassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito tiṃsatikappambhi paṭisaṅkhārasavahayā 
 sattarananasampannā terasa cakkavattino  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sudhāpiṇḍiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sudhāpiṇḍiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    idammattanti  sīmu 
  
               
  
     sucintitattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       tissassa lokanāthassa suddhāpiṭha  madāsahaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena buddhassādiccabandhuno  
  
       aṭṭatiṃse ito kappe rājā āsiṃ mahāruci  
 bhogo ca vipulo āsi sayanaṃ ca anappakaṃ  
  
       piṭhaṃ buddhassa datvāna vippasannena cetasā  
 anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatamattano  
  
              
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pīṭhamadadiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi piṭhadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       aṭṭhatiṃse ito kappe tayo te cakakvattino  
 ruci uparuci ceva mahāruci tatiyako  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucintito thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sucintitattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     aḍḍhacelakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       tissassāhaṃ bhagavato upaḍḍhadussamadāsahaṃ  
 paramakāpaññapattomhi  duggandhena  samappapito  
  
       upaḍḍhadussaṃ datvāna kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ  
 avasesesu kappesu kusalaṃ kāritaṃ  mayā  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ dussamadadiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dussadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekunapaṇṇe  kappamhi rājāno cakkavattino  
 samannacchadanā  nāma khattiṃsāsuṃ janādhipā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aḍḍhacelako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  aḍḍhacelakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
    pubbe piṭha     sudhāpiṭha  simu    kāruñña  syā se    duggatena  machasaṃ    tiritaṃ        ekuṇapaññāsa  sīmu    samantaodanā     se  
  
               
  
     sucidāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kammārohaṃ pure āsiṃ bandhumāyaṃ puruttame  
 sucidānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vipassissa mahesino  
  
       vajiraggasamaṃ ñāṇaṃ hoti kammena tādisā   
 virāgomhi vimuttomhi pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ  
  
              
  
       anite ca bhave sabbe vattamāne canāgate  
 ñāṇena viciniṃ sabbaṃ sucidānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe sattāsuṃ vajiravahayā   
 sattarananasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sucinadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     gandhamāliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato gandhathupaṃ akāsahaṃ  
 sumanehi paṭicchannaṃ buddhānucchavikaṃ kataṃ  
  
       kañcakanagghiyasaṅkāsaṃ buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ  
 indivaraṃva jalitaṃ ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ  
  
       vyagghusabhaṃva pavaraṃ abhijātaṃva kesariṃ  
 nisinnaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ bhikkhusaṃghapurakkhataṃ  
 canditvā satthuno pāde pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho  
  
       catunavute ito kappe gandhamālaṃ yato adaṃ  
 buddhe katassa kārassa phalenāhaṃ visesato  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       cattārisambhi ekune kappe āsiṃsu soḷasa  
 devagandhasanāmā te rājāno cakkavattano  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhamāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  gandhamāliyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
    tādisaṃ  sabbattha    vajirāsamā     se    ahaṃ     se 
  
               
              
  
     tipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ  
 pāṭaliṃ haritaṃ disvā tīṇi pupphāni okiriṃ  
  
       sanna  patatāni gaṇhitvā bahi chaḍḍhesahaṃ tadā  
 antosuddhaṃ bahisuddhaṃ suvimuttaṃ anāsavaṃ  
  
       sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 pāṭaliṃ abhivadetvā tattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ bodhimabhipujayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhipujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       samantapāsādikā nāma resāsiṃsu rājino  
 ito tettiṃsakappamhi cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     madhupiṇḍikattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipine  kānane disvā appasadde nirākule  
 siddhatthaṃ isinaṃ seṭṭhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
  
       nibbutattaṃ  mahānāgaṃ nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā  
 osadhiṃva virocantaṃ devasaṅghanamassitaṃ  
 vitti me pahutā āsi  ñāṇaṃ uppajji tāvade  
  
       vuṭṭhitassa samādhimhā madhuṃ datvāna satthuno  
 vanditvā satthuno pāde pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho  
  
              
  
       catuttiṃsambhi kappamhi rājā āsiṃ sudassano  
 madhu bhisehi samati bhojanambhi ca tāvade  
 madhuvassaṃ pavassittha pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ madhuṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catuttiṃse ito kappe cattāro te sudassanā  
 sattaratanampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā madhupiṇḍiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  madhupiṇḍikattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
    satta  sīmu patita  machasaṃ sukkhapaṇṇāni  syā    vicane        nibabutaṃ taṃ  se    mamāhu tāvade  machasaṃ me pāhuṇā tāva  simu  
  
               
  
     senāsanadāyakattherāpadaṃ  
  
       siddhathessa bhagavato adāsiṃ paṇaṇasattharaṃ  
 samantā upahāraṃ  ca kusumaṃ okiriṃ ahaṃ  
  
       pāsādevaṃ guṇaṃ  rammaṃ  anubhomi mahārahaṃ   
 mahagghāni ca pupphāni sayanebhisavanti  me  
  
       sayanehaṃ tuvaṭṭāmi vicitte pupphasanthate  
 pupphavuṭṭhi ca sayane abhivassati tāvade  
  
       catunavute ito kappe adāsiṃ paṇṇasantharaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi santharassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tiṇasattharakā nāma sattete cakakvattino  
 ito te pañcame kappe uppajjiṃsu janādhipā  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā senāsanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  senāsanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     veyyāvaccakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipassissa bhagavato mahābhurigaṇo  ahu  
  
       deyyadhammo ca me natthi sugatassa mahesino  
 avandiṃ satthuno pāde vippasannena cetasā  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe veyyāvaccaṃ akāsahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi veyyāvaccassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito ca aṭṭhame kappe rājā āsiṃ sucintito  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā veyyāvaccako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  veyyāvaccakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      buddhupaṭṭhākattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipassino bhagavato ahosiṃ saṃkhadhammako  
 niccupaṭṭhānayuttomhi sugatassa mahesino  
  
       upaṭṭhānaphalaṃ passa lokanāthassa tādino  
 saṭṭhi turiyasahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā  
  
    upakāriṃ     upakāri  te    pāsāde ca guhaṃ     se pāsāde caturo  the    ramme  the    mahārahe  the    sayanebhiharanti  the    mahāpugagaṇo  simu machasaṃ     theragāthaṭṭhakāyaṃ sañajayattheranāmena dasasitaṃ  
  
               
              
  
       ekanavute ito kappe upaṭṭhahiṃ mahāisiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catuvise  ito kappe mahānigeghāsanāmakā  
 soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhupaṭṭhāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  buddhapaṭṭhākattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 sudhāsucinti celañca suci ca gandhamāliyo  
 tipupphiyo madhu senā  ceyyāvacco cupaṭṭhako   
 samasaṭṭhi ca gāthāyo asmiṃ vagge pakittitā  
  sudhāpiṇḍiyavaggo dasamo   
  
 atha vagguddānaṃ  
 buddhavaggo hi paṭhamo sihāsana subhūti ca  
 kuṇḍadhāno upāli ca vijani sakacinti ca  
 nāgasamālo timiro sudhāvaggena te dasa  
 catuddasasataṃ gāthā pañcapaññāsameva ca  
  buddhavaggadasakaṃ  
 paṭhamasatakaṃ samattaṃ 
  
              
  
      bhikkhādāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇaṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
 pavanā abhinikkhantaṃ vanā nibbanamāgataṃ  
  
       kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ pādāsiṃ siddhatthassa mahesino  
 paññassa  upasantassa mahāvīrassatādino  
  
       padenānupadaṃ yantaṃ  nibabāpente  mahājanaṃ  
 uḷārā vitti me jātā buddhe ādiccabandhuti  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattāsitimhito kappe mahāreṇusanāmakā  
 sattaratanasampannā satteva cakkavattino  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhikkhādāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  bhikkhādāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    catunavute        ca dhammako        paññāya  simu    yanto  simu    nibbāpentaṃ        vitti me pāhuṇā tāva buddhassādiccabandhuno  syā    se    bandhune  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      ñāṇasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā  
 tidhā pabhinnamātaṅgaṃ kuñajaraṃva mahesinaṃ  
  
       obhāsantaṃ disā sabbā uḷurājaṃva puritaṃ  
 rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ apassisaṃ  
  
       ñāṇe cittaṃ pasādetvā paggahetvāna añjaliṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano siddhatthaṃ abhivādayiṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ñāṇasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tesattatimbhito kappe soḷasāsuṃ naruttamā  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ñāṇasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ñāṇasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      uppalahatthittherāpadānaṃ  
  
       tivarāyaṃ nivāsihaṃ ahosiṃ māliko tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ siddhatthaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       pasannacitto sumano pupphahatthamadāsahaṃ  
 yattha yatthupapajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasā  
  
       anubhomi phalaṃ iṭṭhaṃ pubbe sukatamattano  
 parikkhitto sumallehi pupphadānassidaṃ  phalaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catunavutupādāya ṭhapetvā vattamānakaṃ  
 pañcarājasatā tattha najjupama  sanāmakā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uppalahatthiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  uppalahatthiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
    ajassihaṃ  simu    sasaññāya     se    najjasama  machasaṃ se 
  
               
  
      padapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato jātipupphamadāsahaṃ  
 pādesu sattapupphāni hāsenokiritāni  me  
  
       tena kammenahaṃ ajja atibhomi narāmare  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane  
  
              
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       samantagandhanāmāsuṃ terasa cakkavattino  
 ito pañcamake kappe cāturāntā janādhipā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  padapujakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      muṭṭhipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       sudassanoti nāmena mālākāro ahaṃ tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       jātipupphaṃ gahevona pujayiṃ padumuttaraṃ  
 visuddhacakkhu sumano dibbacakkhuṃ samajjhagaṃ  
  
       etissā pupphapujāya cittassa paṇidhihi ca  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjati  
  
       soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno devuttarasanāmakā  
 chattiṃsamhi ito kappe cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā muṭṭhipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  muṭṭhipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
    hāsena kāritāni     hāsenākiritāni  the    gaṇadhipā     se 
  
               
  
      udakapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ gacchantaṃ anilañajase  
 ghatāsanaṃva jalitaṃ ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ  
  
       pāṇinā udakaṃ gayha ākāse ukkhipiṃ  
 sampaṭicchi mahāvīro buddho kāruṇiko isi  
  
              
  
       antalikkhe ṭhito satthā padumuttaranāmako  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha  
  
       iminedakadānena pitiuppādanena ca  
 kappasatasahassamhi  duggatiṃ nupapajjati  
  
       tena kammena dipadinde lokajeṭṭhe narāsabhe  
 pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
       sahassarājanāmena tayo te cakkavattino  
 pañcasaṭṭhi kappasate cāturantā janādhipā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  udakapūjakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      naḷamāliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 tiṇatthare  nisinnassa upasantassa tādino  
  
       naḷamālaṃ gahetvāna bandhitvā vijaniṃ ahaṃ  
 buddhassa upanāmesiṃ dipadindassa tādino  
  
       paṭiggahetvā sabbaññu vijaniṃ lokanāyako  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha  
  
       yathā me kāyo nibbāti pariḷāho na vijjati  
 tatheva tividhaggihi cittaṃ tava vimuccatu 
  
       sabbe devā samāgacchuṃ ye keci vananissitā  
 sossāma buddhavacanaṃ hāsayantaṃ ca dāyakaṃ 
  
       nisinno bhagavā tattha devasaṃghapurakkhato  
 dāyakaṃ sampahaṃsento imā gāthā abhāsatha  
  
    mayi     se    sahassamhi  machasaṃ    nupagacchati        tiṇannare     se tiṇasatthare  the    dumanissitā     se  
  
               
  
       iminā vijanidānena cittassa paṇidhihi ca  
 subbato nāma nāmena cakakvatti bhavissati  
  
              
  
       tena kamamāvasesena sukkamūlena codito  
 māluto nāma nāmena cakkavatti bhavissati  
  
       iminā vijanidānena sammānavipulena ca  
 kappasatasahassamhi duggatiṃ nupapajjati 
  
       tiṃsakappasahassamhi subbatā aṭṭhatiṃsa te  
 ekunatiṃsahasse aṭṭha mālutanāmakā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷamāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  naḷamāliyattherassa apadānaṃ  sattamaṃ   
 sattamabhāṇavāraṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
  
      āsanupaṭṭhāpakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kānanaṃ vanamogayha appasaddaṃ nirākulaṃ  
 sihāsanaṃ mayā dinnaṃ atthadassissa tādino  
  
       mālahatthaṃ gahetvāna katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ  
 satthāraṃ payirupāsitvā pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho  
  
       tena kammena dipadinde lokajeṭṭhe narāsabhe  
 sannibbāpemi attānaṃ  bhavā sabbe samuhatā  
  
       aṭṭhārase  kappasate yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sihāsanasasidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito satatakappasate sannibbāpaka khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āsanupaṭṭhāpaka  thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  āsanupaṭṭhāpakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    naḷamāliya therassāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ    sannibbāpesimattānaṃ  se    aṭṭārasa  machasaṃ    āsanupaṭṭhāhaka  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      biḷālidāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       himavantassa avidūre vasāmi paṇṇasatthare  
 ghāsesu gedhamāpanno seyyasilo vahaṃ tadā  
  
       khaṇāntālu kalambāni biḷāni nakkalāni ca  
 kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ billaṃ ābhitvā  paṭiyāditaṃ  
  
       padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya āgacchi mama santikaṃ  
  
       upāgataṃ mahānāgaṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 biḷāliṃ paggahetvāna pattamhi okiriṃ ahaṃ  
  
       paribhuñaji mahāvīro tosayanetatā mamaṃ tadā  
 paribhuñajitvāna sabbaññu imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha  
  
       sakaṃ cittaṃ padādetvā biḷāliṃ me adā tuvaṃ  
 kappānaṃ satasahasasaṃ duggatiṃ nupagacchasi  
  
       catupaññāsito kappe sumekhaliya savahayo    
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       carimaṃ vattate mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā biḷādāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  biḷādāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
              
  
      reṇupajakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ sataraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ  
 obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā uḷurājaṃva puritaṃ  
  
       purakkhataṃ sāvakehi sāgareheva  mediniṃ  
 nāgaṃ paggayha reṇuhi vipassissā bhiropayiṃ  
  
       ekavute ito kappe yaṃ reṇumabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    āhatvā  simu āharitvā se    nupapajjasi  machasaṃ se  ayaṃ gāthā asmiṃ apadāne aṭṭhamagāthāvasena sihalakkharamudadita potthake dissati     sāgareneva     se 
  
               
  
       paṇṇanālisito kappe reṇu nāmāsi khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā reṇupujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  reṇupujakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ  
 uddānaṃ  
 bhikkhādāyī ñāṇasaññi hatthiyo padapujako  
 muṭṭhipupphi udakado naḷamāli upaṭṭhako  
 biḷālidāyī reṇu ca gāthāyo cha ca saṭṭhi ca  
  bhikkhādāyivaggo ekādasamo   
  
      mahāparivarattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipassi nāma bagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 aṭṭhasaṭṭisahassehi pāvisi bandhumaṃ tadā  
  
       nagarā abhinikkhamma agamaṃ dipacetiyaṃ  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
  
       cullāsitisahassāni yakkā mayhaṃ upanitike  
 upaṭṭhahanti sakkaccaṃ indaṃva tidasā gaṇā  
  
              
  
       bhavanā abhinikkhamma dussaṃ paggayhahaṃ tadā  
 sirasā abhivādesiṃ taṃ vādāsiṃ mahesino  
  
       aho buddho aho dhammo  aho no santhusampadā 
 buddhassa ānubhāvena vasudhāyaṃ pakampatha  
  
       taṃ ca acchariyaṃ disvā abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ  
 buddhe citataṃ pasādesiṃ dipadindamhi tādine  
  
       sohaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā dussaṃ datvāna satthuno  
 saraṇañca upāgañachiṃ sāmacco saparijjano 
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kamamamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito paṇṇarase kappe soḷasāsuṃ suvāhanā  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāparivāro thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  mahāparivārattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    nivāsako se       aho dhammā  simu  mahāparivārakattheraapadānaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      sumaṅgalattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       atthadassī jinavaro lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 vihārā abhinikkhamma taḷākaṃ upasaṅkami  
  
       nahātvā pitvā ca sambuddho uttaritvekacivaro  
 aṭṭhāsi bhagavā tattha vilokento disodisaṃ  
  
       bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena appoṭhesiṃ ahaṃ tadā  
  
       sataraṃsiṃvava jotantaṃ pabhāsantaṃva kañcanaṃ  
 nacce gite ca yuttohaṃ  pañcaṅgaturiyambhi ca  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 sabbe satte atibhomi vipulo hoti me yaso  
  
              
  
       namo te purisājañña nāmo te purisuttama  
 attānaṃ tosayitvāna pare tosesi tvaṃ mune 
  
       pariggayha  nisīditvā hāsaṃ katvāna subbate    
 upaṭṭhahitvā sambuddhaṃ tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
       soḷaseto kappasate davi nava ekacintitā  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumaṅgalo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sumaṅgalattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      saraṇagamaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       ubhinnaṃ devarājunaṃ saṅgāmo paccupaṭṭhito  
 ahosi samupabbuḷho mahāghoso pavatatatha  
  
       padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggabho  
 antaḷikkhe ṭhito satthā saṃvejesi mahājanaṃ  
  
       sabbe devā attamanā nikkhittakavacāvudhā  
 sambuddhambhivādetvā ekaggāsiṃsu tāvade  
  
    naccagite payuntohaṃ  machasaṃ    pañcaturiyasatamhi ca     paṭiggahetvā    se pariggahe  machasaṃ    subbato  simu    saṅgāmo samupaṭṭhito  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       amhaṃ saṅkappamaññāya vācāsabhimudirayī  
 anukampako lokamidu nibbāpesi mahājanaṃ  
  
       paduṭṭhacitto manujo ekapāṇaṃ  ciheṭhayaṃ  
 tena cittappadosena apāyaṃ upapajjati  
  
       saṅgāmasise nāgova bahu pāṇe viheṭhayaṃ  
 nibbāpetha sakaṃ cittaṃ mā haññittho punappunaṃ 
  
       dvinnampi yakkarājunaṃ senāyo vimhitā ahu  
 saraṇañca upāgacchuṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ sutādinaṃ  
  
              
  
       saññāpetvāna janataṃ uddhari pana  cakkhumā  
 pekkhamānova devehi pakkāmi uttarāmukho  
  
       paṭhamaṃ saranaṃ gañachiṃ  dipadindassa tādino  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ  
  
       mahādundubhināmā ca  loḷasāsuṃ rathesabhā  
 tiṃsakappasahassambhi rājāno cakkavattino 
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saraṇagamaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  saraṇagamaniyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      ekāsanisattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       varuṇo nāma nāmena devarājā ahaṃ tadā  
 upaṭṭhahesiṃ sambuddhaṃ sayoggabalavāhano  
  
       nibbute lokatāthambhi atthadassinaruttame  
 turiyaṃ sabbamādiya agamaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ  
  
       vāditena ca naccena sammatālasamāhito  
 sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ upaṭṭhiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ  
  
       upaṭṭhahitvā taṃ bodhiṃ dharaṇiruhapādapaṃ  
 pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
       sakakammābhiraddhohaṃ pasanno bodhimuttame  
 tena cittappasādena nimmānaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
    pāṇi  simu    padamuddhari  machasaṃ    gacchiṃ  machasaṃ    mahāsucindāhi nāma     
  
               
  
       saṭṭhi turiyasahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā  
 manussesu ca devesu vattamānaṃ bhavābhavo  
  
       subāhu nāma nāmena catuttiṃsāsu khattiyā 
 sattaratanasampanno pañca kappasate ito 
  
              
  
       tividhaggi nibbutā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekāsaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ekāsaniyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      suvaṇṇapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipassi nāma bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 nisinno janakāyassa deseti amataṃ padaṃ  
  
       tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna dipadindassa tādino  
 soṇṇapupphāni cattari buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇacchadanaṃ āsi yāvatā parisā tadā  
 buddhābhā ca suvaṇṇāhā āloko vipulo ahu  
  
       udaggacitto sumano vedajāto katañajali  
 vittisañajanano tesaṃ diṭṭhadhammasukhāvaho  
  
       āyācitvāna sambuddhaṃ vanditvāna ca subbataṃ  
 pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna sakaṃ bhavanupāgamiṃ  
  
       bhavane upaviṭṭhohaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussariṃ  
 tena cittappasādena tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno nemata nāmakā  
 tetāḷise ito kappe cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā suvaṇṇapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  suvaṇṇapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
               
              
  
      citakapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       casāmi rājāyatane sāmacco saparijjano  
 parinibbute bhagavati sikine lokabandhune  
  
       pasannacitto sumano citakaṃ agamāsahaṃ  
 turiyaṃ tattha vādetvā gandhamālaṃ samokiriṃ  
  
       citambhi pujaṃ katvāna  vanditvā citakaṃ ahaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano sakaṃ bhavanupāgamiṃ  
  
       bhavano upaviṭṭhohaṃ citapujaṃ  anussariṃ  
 tena kammena dipadinde lokajeṭṭhe narāsabhe  
  
       anubhovona sampattiṃ devesu manujesu ca  
 patetāmbhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvāna jayaparājayaṃ  
  
       ekaniṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabharopayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi citapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekūnatiṃse kappamhi ito soḷasa rājāno    
 uggatā nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  citakapajakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
      buddhasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       yadā vipassi lokaggo āyusaṃkhāramossaji  
 paṭhavi sampakampittha medini jalamekhalā  
  
       otataṃ vitthataṃ  mayhaṃ suvicittavaṭaṃsakaṃ    
 bhavanampi pakampittha buddhassa āyusaṃkhaye  
  
              
  
       taso mayhaṃ samuppanno bhavane sampakampite  
 uppāto  nu kimatthāya āloko vipulo ahu  
  
       vessavaṇo idhāgamma nibbāpesī mahājanaṃ  
 pāṇabhute bhayaṃ natthi ekaggā hotha saṃvutā  
  
       aho buddho aho dhammo  no satthu sampadā  
 yasmiṃ upapajjamānambhi paṭhavi sampakampati 
  
       buddhānubhāvaṃ kittetvā kappaṃ saggambhi modahaṃ  
 avasesesu kappesu kusalaṃ caritaṃ   mayā  
  
    sikhino lokabandhuno simu syā    citaka pujaṃ katvā     se    citakapujaṃ  simu    rājino  simu    cittaṃ  se       suvicittaṃ     se    uppādo  sabbattha    pāṇabhūtaṃ    se    dhammo  itipi     kāritaṃ     se karitaṃ  simu  
  
               
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito cuddasakappamhi rājā āsiṃ patāpavā  
 yamito nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  buddhasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      maggasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa sāvakā vanacārino  
 vippanaṭṭhā buhāraññe andhāva anusuyare  
  
       anussaritvā sambuddhaṃ padumuttaranāmakaṃ  
 tassa te munino puttā vippanaṭṭhā mahāvane  
  
       bhavanā oruhitvāna agamaṃ bhikkhusantikaṃ   
 tesaṃ maggañca ācikkhiṃ bhojanañca adāsahaṃ  
  
       tena kammena dipadinde lokajeṭṭhe narāsabhe  
 jātiyā sattavassohaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ  
  
       sacakkhu nāma nāmena dvādasa cakkavattino  
 sattaratanasampannā pañcakappasate ito  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maggasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  maggasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
      paccupaṭṭhānasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       atthadassimhi sugate nibbute samanantarā  
 yakkhayoniṃ upapajajiṃ yasaṃ patetā cahaṃ tadā  
  
       dulladdhaṃ vata me āsiṃ duppabhātaṃ duruṭṭhitaṃ  
 yaṃ me bhoge vijjamāne parinibbāyi cakkhumā  
  
    santite     se 
  
               
  
       mama saṅkappamaññāya sāgaro nāma sāvako  
 mamuddharitukāmo so āgacci mama santikaṃ  
  
       ninnu socasi mā bhāsi cara dhammaṃ  sumedhasa  
 anuppadinnā buddhena sabbesaṃ bijasampadā  
  
       yo ca pujeyya sambuddhaṃ tiṭṭantaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 dhātuṃ sāsapamatataṃ hi nibbutassāpi pujaye  
  
       same cittappasādambhi samaṃ puññaṃ mahaggataṃ  
 tasmā thupaṃ karitvāna pujehi jinadhātuyo 
  
       sāgarassa vaco sutvā buddhathupaṃ akāsahaṃ  
 pañca vasse paricariṃ munino thupamuttamaṃ  
  
       tena kammena dipadinde lokajeṭṭhe narāsabhe  
 sampattiṃ anubhotvāna arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ  
  
       bhuripaññā ca cattāro sattakappasate ito  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paccupaṭṭhānasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  paccupaṭṭhānasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
              
  
      jātipujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       jāyantassa vipassissa aloko vipulo ahu  
 paṭhavi ca pakampittha sasāgarā  sapabbatā  
  
       nemittā ca viyākaṃsu budho loke bhavissati  
 aggo ca sabbasattānaṃ janataṃ uddharissati  
  
       nemittānaṃ suṇitvāna jātipujamakāsahaṃ  
 edisā pujanā natthi yādisā jātipujanā  
  
       saṃvaritvāna  kusalaṃ sakaṃ citataṃ pasādayiṃ  
 jātipujaṃ karitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
    santike     se the    varadhamma  se    sasāgara  simu    saṃsaritvāna     se saṃharitvāna  simu 
  
               
  
       yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 sabbe satte anibhomi jātipujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       dhāniyo  maṃ upaṭṭhanti mama citatavasānugā  
 na tā  sakkonta kopetuṃ jātipujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pujakamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi jātipujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       supāricāriyā nāma catuttiṃsa janādhipā  
 ito tatiyakappamhi cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jātipujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  jātipujakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 parivāra sumaṅgalā saraṇāsana pupphakā  
 citapuji buddhasaññi maggupaṭṭhāna jātinā  
 gāthāyo navuti vuttā gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi  
  mahāparivāravaggo dvādasamo   
  
              
  
      sereyyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragu  
 abbhokāse ṭhito santo addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       sihaṃ yathā vanacaraṃ vyaggharājaṃva titatasaṃ  
 tidhā pabhinnamātaṅgaṃ kuñajaraṃva mahesinaṃ  
  
       sereyyakaṃ gahetvāna ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ  
 buddhassa ānubhāvena parivārenti sabbato  
  
       adhiṭṭāsi mahāvīro sabbaññu lokanāyako  
 samantā pupphacchadanā  okiriṃsu nāsabhaṃ  
  
       tato sā pupphakañcukā  antovaṇṭā bahimukhā  
 sattāhaṃ chadanaṃ hutvā   tato antaradhāyatha  
  
    dhātuyo ca  se       te        sabbaso  machasaṃ    jadanaṃ     se    sapuppha        katvā  simu 
  
               
  
       taṃ ca acchariyaṃ disvā abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ  
 buddhe cittaṃ pasādesiṃ sugate lokanāyake  
  
       tena cittappasādena sukkamūlena codito  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ  
  
       paṇṇarasasahassambhi kappānaṃ pañcavisa te  
 cittamālāsanāmaṃ  ca cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sereyyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  serayyekattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
      pupphathupiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       himavantassā vidure kukkuṭo  nāma pabbato  
 vemajjhe tassa vasati bruhmaṇomantapāragu  
  
       pañca sissasahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā  
 pubbuṭṭhāyi ca te āsuṃ mantesu ca visāradā  
  
              
  
       buddho loke samuppanno taṃ vijānātha no bhavaṃ  
 asitā vyañajanānassa khattiṃsa varalakkhaṇā  byāmappabho jinavaro ādiccova virocati  
  
       sissānaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā buhmaṇo mantapāragu  
 assamā abhinikkhamma disaṃ pucchati sissake  
 yambhi dese mahaviro vasati lokanāyako  
  
       tāhaṃ disaṃ namassissaṃ  jinaṃ appaṭipuggalaṃ  
 udaggacitto sumano pujesiṃ  taṃ tathāgataṃ  
  
       etha sissā gamissāma dakkhissāmatathāgataṃ  
 vanditvā santhuno pāde sossama jinasāsanaṃ  
  
       ekāhaṃ abhinikkhamma vyādhiṃ paṭilabhiṃ ahaṃ  
 vyādhinā piḷito santo sālaṃ vesayituṃ  gamiṃ  
  
       sabbe sisse samānetvā apucchiṃ te tathāgataṃ   
 kidisaṃ lokanāthassa guṇaṃ paramabuddhino  
  
    vinamālā     citamālā  machasaṃ    kukkuro  machasaṃ    brāhmaṇo     se    nahi disvāna passissaṃ        pujessaṃ ca        co seyituṃ  simu    tathā ahaṃ     se 
  
               
  
       te me puṭṭhā vyākariṃsu yathā dassācino tathā  
 sakkaccaṃ  buddhaseṭṭhaṃ taṃ dassesuṃ mama sammukhā  
  
       tesāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 pupphehi thupaṃ katvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
       te me sarīraṃ jhāpetvā agamuṃ  buddhasantike  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna satthāraṃ abhivādayuṃ  
  
       pupphehi thupaṃ katvāna sugatassamahesino  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ  
  
       cattārisasahassamhi kappe soḷasa khattiyā  
 nāmenaggisamā nāma cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       vise kappasahassamhi rājāno cakkavattino  
 ghatāsanasanāmā ca aṭṭhatiṃsa mahipati  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphipiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pupphapiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
              
  
      pāyāsadāyaka ttherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ  khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ    
 pavanā abhinikkhantaṃ bhikkhusaṃghapurakkhataṃ  
  
       mahaccā  kaṃsapātiyā vaḍḍhetvā pāyasaṃ ahaṃ  
 āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmo so upanesiṃ  baliṃ ahaṃ  
  
       bhagavā tambhi samaye lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 caṅkamaṃ susamāruḷho ambare anilāyane  
  
       taṃ ca acchariyaṃ disva abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ  
 ṭhapayitvā kaṃsapātiṃ vipassiṃ abhivādayiṃ  
  
       tuvaṃ devosi sabbaññu sadeve sahamānuse  
 anukampaṃ upādāya paṭigaṇha mahāmuni  
  
       paṭiggahesi bhagavā sababaññu lokanāyako  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke mahāmuni    
  
    kukkuṭṭha        agamaṃsu     se  pāyasadāyaka  machasaṃ    suvaṇṇavaṇṇo samubuddhe  machasaṃ    lakkhaṇo abhinikkhanto purakkhato  machasaṃ   sahatthā     se    agamāsiṃ     se 
  
               
  
       ekanavute ito kappeyaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pāyāsassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekatāḷisito kappe buddho nāmāsi khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāyāsadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pasāyadāyakottherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      gandhodakiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       nisajja pāsādavera vipassiṃ addasaṃ jinaṃ  
 kakudhaṃ vilasantaṃva sabbaññuṃ tamanāsakaṃ  
  
       pāsādassāvidure ca gacchati lokanāyako  
 pabhā niddhāvate tassa yathā ca 
  
              
  
       gandhodakañca paggayha buddhaseṭṭhaṃ samokiriṃ  
 tena cittappasādena tattha kālanato ahaṃ  
  
       ekatāḷisito kappe yaṃ gandhodakamākiriṃ     
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe sugandho nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhodakiyo  thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  gandhodakiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      sammukhātthavikattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       jāyamāne vipassimhi nimittaṃ vyākariṃ ahaṃ  
 nibbāpayañca janataṃ buddho loke bhavissati  
  
       yasmiñca jāyamānasmiṃ dasasahassi pakampati  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
       yasmiñca jāyamānasmiṃ āloko vipulo ahu  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
    sabbaññutamanāsavaṃ        sataraṃsimbhi nibabute     se syā    gandhodakaṃ samokiriṃ     se gandhodakamokiriṃ syā  sugandhodakiyo  simu 
  
               
  
       yasmiṃ ca jāyamānasmiṃ saritāyo na sandisuṃ  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
       yasmiṃ ca jāyamānasmiṃ avicaggi na pajjali  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
       yasmiṃ ca jāyamānasmiṃ pakkhisaṃgho na sañcari  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
       yasmiṃ ca jāyamānasmiṃ vātakkhandho na vāyati  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
       yasmiṃ ca jāyamānasmiṃ sabbaratanāni jotisuṃ  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
       yasmiṃ ca jāyamānasmiṃ sattāsuṃ padavikkamā  
 sodāni bhagavā satthā dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
              
  
       jātamatto ca sambuddho disā sabbā vilokayi  
 vācāsabhimudiresi esā buddhāna dhammatā  
  
       saṃvejayitvā janataṃ thavitvāna lokanāyakaṃ  
 sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho  
  
       ekanavute ito  kappe yaṃ buddhamahithomayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thomanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito navutikappambhi sammukhāthavikavhayo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭhavidunduhi  nāma ekunanavutimbhito  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       aṭṭhāsitimbhito kappe obhāso nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       sattāsitimbhito kappe saritacchedanavhayo  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       agginibbāpano nāma kappānaṃ chaḷasitiyā  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       gatipacchedano nāma kappānaṃ pañcasitiyā  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       rājā vātasamo nāma kappānaṃ cullasitiyā  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       ratanapajjalo nāma kappānaṃ teasitiyā  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
    sattesu     se    ekanavutito  machasaṃ    paṭhavidunduhi  katthavi  
  
               
  
       padavikkamano nāma kappānaṃ dveasitiyā  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       rājā vilokano nāma kappānaṃ ekasitiyā  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       girisāroti nāmena kappesitimhi khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanona cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sammukhāthaviko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sammukhāthavikattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
              
  
      kusumāsaniyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       nagare dhaññavatiyā ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadā  
 lakkhaṇe itihāse ca sanighaṇḍu sakeṭubhe  
  
       padako veyyākaraṇo  nimitte kovido ahaṃ  
 manneta ca sisse vācesiṃ tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragu  
  
       pañca uppalahatthāni piṭhiyaṃ  ṭhapitāni me  
 āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmohaṃ pitumātusamāgame  
  
       tadā vipassi bhagavā bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato  
 obhāsentā disā sabbā āgacchati narāsabho  
  
       āsanaṃ paññapetvāna nimantetvā mahāmuniṃ  
 santharitvāna taṃ pupphaṃ abhinesiṃ  sakaṃ gharaṃ  
  
       yaṃ me atthi sake gehe āmisaṃ paccupaṭṭhitaṃ  
 tāhaṃ buddhassa pādisiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       bhuttāviṃ kālamaññāya pupphahatthaṃ  adāsahaṃ  
 anumoditvāna sababaññu pakkāmi uttarāmukho  
  
       ekanavute ito  kappe yaṃ pupphamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphādānassaidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       anantarā ito kappe rājāhuṃ varadassano  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kusumāsaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  kusumāsaniyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
    padake  veyyākaraṇe  simu    piṭṭhiyaṃ  machasaṃ       atinesiṃ  si mu    ekahatthaṃ     se    ekanavutito  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      phaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ajjhāyako ntadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragu  
 bhimavantassāvidure vasāmi assame ahaṃ  
  
       aggihuttañca me atthi puṇḍarikaphalāni ca  
 puṭake nikkhipitvāna dumagge laggitaṃ mayā  
  
              
  
       padumuttaro lokavidu āhutitaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mamuddharitukāmo so bhikkhanto maṃ upāgami  
  
       pasannacitto sumano phalaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ  
 vittisañajanano mayhaṃ diṭṭhadhammasukhāvaho  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇo sambuddho āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho  
 antalikkhe ṭhito satthā satthā imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha  
  
       iminā phaladānena cetanā paṇidhihi ca  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggati nupagacchati
