 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā avyādhiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  avyādhikattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
      aṅkolapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       nārado iti me nāmaṃ kassapo iti maṃ vidu  
 addasaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ vipassiṃ devasakkataṃ  
  
       anubyañajanadharaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
 aṅkolapupphaṃ paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catusattatito kappe romaso nāma khattiyo  
 āmuttamālābharaṇo sayoggabavāhato  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aṅkolapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  aṅkolapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
  abyādhika  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      sovaṇṇavaṭaṃsakiyayattherāpadānaṃ   
  
       uyyānabhumiṃ niyyanto addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 vaṭaṃsakaṃ gahetvāna sovaṇṇaṃ sādhunimmitaṃ  
  
       sighaṃ tato samoruyha  hatthikkhanvadhagato ahaṃ  
 buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sikhino lokabandhuno  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ    
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattavise ito kapepa eko āsiṃ janādhipo  
 mahāpatāpa nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sovaṇṇavaṭaṃsakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sovaṇṇavaṭaṃsakiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      miñajavaṭaṃsakiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       nibbute lokanāthambhi sikhimhi vadataṃ vare  
 vaṭaṃsakehi ākiṇṇaṃ bodhipujamakāsahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhipujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito chabbisatikappe ahuṃ meghabbha nāmako  
 sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā miñajavaṭaṃsakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  miñajavaṭaṃsakiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
              
  
      sukatāveliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       asitonāma nāmena mālākāro ahuṃ  tadā  
 āvelaṃ paggahevona rañño dātuṃ vajāmahaṃ  
  
       asampattamhi rājānaṃ addasaṃ sikhināyakaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse  ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
  vaṭaṃsakiyattherāpadānaṃ simu    samāruyha  machasaṃ    pupphamabhiropayiṃ  machasaṃ   pupphapujāyidaṃ  machasaṃ    ahaṃ  machasaṃ    ekattiṃse  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       pañcavise ito kappe rājāhosiṃ mahabbalo  
 vehāro nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sukatāveliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sukatāveliyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      ekavandiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       usabhaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ vessabhuṃ vijitāvitaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandihaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       catuvīsatikappamhi vigatānandanāmako  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekavandiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ekavandiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 ālambanañca ajinaṃ maṃsadā rakkhadāyako 
 avyādhi aṅkolaṃ  soṇṇaṃ miñajaṃ āvela vandanaṃ 
 pañcapaññasa gāthāyo gaṇitā atthadassihi  
  ālambanadāyakavaggo tevisatimo   
  
              
  
      udakāsanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       ārāmadvārā nikkhamma phalakaṃ satthariṃ ahaṃ  
 udakañca upaṭṭhāsiṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āsane coke phalaṃ  
  
       ito paṇṇarase kappe abhisāmasamavhayo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
    buddhaseṭṭhamavandahaṃ  machasaṃ    cakulaṃ  syā 
  
               
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakāsanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  udakāsanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
      bhājanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ   
  
       nagare bandhumatiyā kumbhakāro ahaṃ tadā  
 bhājanaṃ anupālesiṃ bhikkhusaṅghassa tāvade  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe bhājanaṃ anupālayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhājanassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tepaññāse ito kappe anantajāli nāmako  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhājanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  bhājanadākattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      sālapupiyattherāpādanaṃ  
  
       aruṇavatiyā nagare ahosiṃ pupiko ahaṃ  
 mama dvārena gacchantaṃ sikhinaṃ addasaṃ jinaṃ  
  
       buddhassa pattaṃ paggayha sālapupaṃ  adāsahaṃ  
 sammaggatassa buddhassa vippasannena cetasā  
  
              
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ khajjakamadāsahaṃ    
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sālapupassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito cuddasakappambhi asosiṃ amitañajalo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sālapupiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sālapupiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
    bhājanapālakattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ    sālapupphaṃ  machasaṃ    yaṃ pupphamabhidāsahaṃ  machasaṃ  sālapupphiyatherāpadānaṃ  simu machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      kilañajadāyakatthorāpadānaṃ  
  
       tivarāyaṃ pure ramme naḷakāro ahaṃ tadā  
 siddhatthe lokapajjote pasannā janatā tahiṃ  
  
       pujatthaṃ lokanāthassa kilañajaṃ pariyesati  
 buddhapujaṃ karontānaṃ kilañajaṃ adadiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito  kappe yaṃ kammakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kilañajassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattasatattikappambhi rājā āsiṃ jutindharo    
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kilañajadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  kilañajadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      vedikārakatthorāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipassino bhagavato bodhiyā pādaputtame  
 pasannacitto sumano kāresiṃ vedikaṃ ahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe karosiṃ vedikaṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       ito ekādase kappe asosiṃ suriyassamo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vedikārako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  vedikārakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
      vaṇṇakāratthorāpadānaṃ 
  
       nagare aruṇavatiyā vaṇṇakāro ahaṃ tadā  
 cetiye dussabhaṇḍāni nātāvaṇṇaṃ rajesahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ vaṇṇaṃ rajayiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vaṇṇadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    catunnavutito kappe  machasaṃ    jaladadharo  machasaṃ    rajemahaṃ  syā 
  
               
  
       ito tevisatikappe candumasāmako   
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vaṇṇākāro thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  vaṇṇakārattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ  
  
      piyālapupphiyatthopadānaṃ  
  
       migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ  
 piyālaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā gatamagge khipiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piyālapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  piyālapupiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
              
  
      ambayāgadākatthorāpadānaṃ  
  
       sake sippe apatthaddho agamaṃ kānanaṃ ahaṃ  
 sambuddhaṃ yantaṃ disvāna ambayāgaṃ adāsahaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ambayāgassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambayāgadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ambayāgadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    vaṇṇasamasanāmako  machasaṃ  candasama  syā 
  
               
  
      jagatikārakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       nibbute lokanāthambhi atthadassi naruttame  
 jagati kāritā mayhaṃ buddhassa thupamuttame  
  
       aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi jāgatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jagatikārako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  jagatikārakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      vāsidāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kammārohaṃ pure āsiṃ tivarāyaṃ puruttame  
 ekā vāsi mayā dinnā sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ  
  
       catunavute  ito kappe yaṃ vāsimadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vāsidānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vāsidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  vāsidākattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
              
  
 uddānaṃ  
 udakāsana bhājanaṃ sālapupi  kilañajako 
 vedikā vaṇṇakāro ca piyāla ambayāgado 
 jagatī vāsidātā ca gāthā tiṃsa ca aṭṭha ca  
  udakāsanavaggo catuvisatimo   
  
      tuvaradāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ  
 bharitvā  tuvaramādāya saṅghassa adadiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tuvarassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tuvaradāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tuvaradākattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    catunnacutitokappe  machasaṃ    sālapupphi sīmu machasaṃ    haritvā  sīmu machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      nāgakesariyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       dhanuṃ advejjhaṃ katvāna vanamajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ  
 kesaraṃ osaṭaṃ  disvā satapattaṃ samuṭṭhitaṃ  
  
       ubho hatthehi paggayha sire katvāna añjaliṃ  
 buddhassa abhiropesiṃ tissassa lokabandhuno  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipajayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tesattatimbhi kappamhi satta kesaranāmakā  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nāgakosariyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  nāgakesariyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ  
  
              
  
      naḷinakesariyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       jātassarassa vemajjhe vasāmi jalakukkuṭo  
 athaddasaṃ  devadevaṃ gacchantama nilañajase  
  
       tuṇḍena kesariṃ  gayha vippasannena cetasā  
 buddhassa abhiropesiṃ tissassa lokabandhuno  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabipujayidaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhajāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tesattatimbhi kappamhi satapattasanāmako   
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷinakesariyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  naḷinakesariyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      viravipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       khiṇāsavasahassehi niyyāti lokanāyako  
 viravipupphaṃ paggayha  buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhipujayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    ogataṃ  machasaṃ    addasāhaṃ machasaṃ    kesaraṃ  syā    sattakesaranāmako  machasaṃ    ciravapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ    viravapupphamādā ya  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā viravipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  viravipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ  
  
      kuṭidhupakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato ahosiṃ kuṭigopako  
 kālena kālaṃ dhupesiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ  phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kuṭidhupeko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  kuṭidhupakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
      pattadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       paramena damathena siddhatthassa mahesino  
 pattadānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ ujubhūtassa tādino  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pattadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pattadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
      dhātupujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       nibbute lokanāthamhi siddhatthamhi naruttame  
 ekā dhātu mayā laddhā dipadindassa  tādino  
  
       tāhaṃ dhātuṃ gahetvāna buddhassādiccabandhuno  
 pañcavasse paricariṃ tiṭṭhantaṃ ca naruttamaṃ  
  
    dhupadānassidaṃ  machasaṃ    dvipadindassa  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dhātuṃ pujayiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhātupaṭṭhahane phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhātupujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  dhātupujakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      sattalipupphapujakattherāpadānaṃ   
  
       satta sattalipupphāni sise katvānahaṃ tadā  
 buddhassa abhiropesiṃ vessabhumbhi naruttame  
  
       ekaniṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ    
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ  phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattalipphapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pasattalipupphujakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
      bambijāliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       padumuttaro nāma jino sayambhu aggapuggalo  
 catusaccaṃ pakāseti dipeti amataṃ padaṃ  
  
       bimbijālikapupphāni  puphu katvānahaṃ tadā  
 buddhassa abhiropesiṃ dipadindassa tādino  
  
       aṭṭhasaṭṭhimhito kappe caturo kiñajakesarā  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavattī mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bimbijāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  bimbijāliyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
    sattalipu pphiyattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ    yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  machasaṃ    buddhapujā yidaṃ  machasaṃ    bimbijālakapupphāni  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      uddāladāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kakusandho nāma nāmena sayambhu aparājito  
 pavanā nikkhamitvāna anuppatto mahānadiṃ  
  
       uddālakaṃ gahetvāna sayambhussa adāsahaṃ  
 saṃyatassujabhūtassa pasannamānaso tadā    
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphabhijujayiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphadānassida phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uddāladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  uddāladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
              
  
 uddānaṃ  
 tuvara nāga naḷinā viravi kuṭidhupako 
 patto dhātu sattaliyo bimbi uddālakena ca 
 sattatiṃsati gāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi  
  tuvaradāyakavaggo pañcavisatimo   
  
      thomakettherāpadānaṃ  
  
       devaloke ṭhito santo vipassissa mahesino  
 dhammaṃ suṇitvā mudito imaṃ vācamabhāsahaṃ  
  
       namo te purisājañña namo te purisuttama  
 bahuṃ janaṃ  tārayasi desento amataṃ padaṃ  
  
       ekanavūte ito kappe yaṃ vācamabhaṇiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thomanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā thomako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  thomakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    uddālakadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ    ahaṃ  machasaṃ    vācaṃ abhāsahaṃ  machasaṃ    bahujjanaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      ekāsanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vijahitvā devavaṇṇaṃ sabhariyo idhāgamiṃ  
 adhikāraṃ kattukāmo buddhaseṭṭhassa sāsane  
  
       devalo nāma nāmena padumuttarasāvako  
 tassa bhikkhā mayā dinnā vippasannena cetasā  
  
       satasahasse ito  kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekāsanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ekāsanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
              
  
      citakapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ānando nāma sambuddho sayambhu aparājito  
 araññe parinibbāyi amanussamhi kānane  
  
       devalokā idhāgantvā citaṃ katvānahaṃ tadā  
 sarīraṃ tattha jhāpesiṃ sakkārañca akāsahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā cittakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  citakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      ticampakapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       himavantassa avidūre vikato  nāma pabbato  
 tassa vemajjhe vasati samaṇo bhāvitindriyo  
  
       disvāna tassopasamaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
 tīṇi campakapupphāni gahetvāna samokiriṃ  
  
    sanasahassino kappe  machasaṃ    himacatantassavidure     citto  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tivampakapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tivampakapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      sattapāṭaliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare  
 sattapāṭalipupphāni buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattapāṭaliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tassapāṭaliyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
              
  
      upāhanadākayattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ahosi candano nāma sambuddhassatrajo tadā  
 ekopāhano mayā dinno bodhiṃ sampajja me tuvaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ yamupāhanaṃ dadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi upāhanassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upāhanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  upāhanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
               
  
      mañajaripujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       mañajirikaṃ karitvāna rathiyaṃ paṭipajjahaṃ  
 addasaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ  
  
       pasannacitto sumano paramāya ca pitiyā  
 ubho hatthehi paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhijujayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito tesattatikappe eko āsiṃ mahipati  
 jotiyo nāma nāmena cakakvatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mañajaripujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  mañajaripujakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      paṇṇadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       pabbate himavantambhi vākaviradhāro ahaṃ  
 aloṇapaṇṇahakkhomhi niyamesu ca saṃvuto  
  
       pātarāse anuppatte siddhattho upagacchi maṃ  
 tāhaṃ buddhassa pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
              
  
       catunavute  ito kappe yaṃ paṇṇamadidaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi paṇṇadānassadaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattavisatikappamhi rājā āsiṃ yadatthiyo   
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paṇṇadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  paṇṇadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    catunavutito  machasaṃ    sadatthiyo  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      kuṭidāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipinacārī sambuddho rukkhamule vasī tadā  
 paṇṇasālaṃ karitvāna adāsiṃ aparājite  
  
       ekanavute ito  kappe yaṃ paṇṇakuṭikaṃ adaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kuṭidānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       aṭṭhavise  ito kappe soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno   
 sabbatthaagivassiti vuccare cakkavattino  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kuṭidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  kuṭidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      aggajapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ    
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatannare  
 obhāsayantaṃ raṃsiyā  sikhitaṃ sikhinaṃ yathā  
  
       aggajaṃ pupphamādāya upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhijujayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       pañcavisatikappambhi ahosiṃ amitavhayo   
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
              
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aggajapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  aggajapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 thomakekāsana citakaṃ campato sattapāṭapi 
 pāhano  mañajarī paṇṇaṃ kuṭido aggapupphiyo 
 gāthāyo gaṇitā  cettha ekatāḷisameva ca  
  thomakavaggo chabbisatimo   
  
    ekanavutito  machasaṃ    aṭṭatiṃse  syā    rājino  simu  aggapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ    raṃsena  syā    amitogato  machasaṃ    pānadhi  machasaṃ    bhaṇitā  simu 
  
               
  
      ākāsukkhipiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ siddhatthaṃ gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe  
 jalajagge duve gayha upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       ekañca pupphaṃ pādesu buddhaseṭṭhassa nikkhipiṃ  
 ekañca pupphaṃ paggayha ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito khattiṃsakappamhi  eko āsiṃ mahipati  
 antalikkhavaro  nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ākāsukkhipiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ākāsukkhipayattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
      telamakkhiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       siddhatthamhi bhagavati nibbutamhi narāsabhe  
 bodhiyā vedikāyāhaṃ telaṃ makkhesiṃ tāvade  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ telaṃ makkhayiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi makkhanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       catuvise ito kappe succhavi nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā telamakkhiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  telamakkhiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      aḍḍhacandiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       tissassa kho bhagavate bodhiyā pādaputtame  
 aḍḍhavandaṃ mayā dinnaṃ dharaṇiruhapādape  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhipujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    chattiṃsakappamhi  machasaṃ    antalikkhakaro  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       paññacavise ito kappe devalo nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aḍḍhavandiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  aḍḍhavanidiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      padipiyattherāpadānaṃ    
  
       devabhuto ahaṃ santo oruyha paṭhaviṃ tadā  
 padipe pañca pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ padipamadaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       pañcapaññāsake kappe eko āsiṃ mahipati  
 samantacakkhu nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padipiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  padipiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
              
  
      biḷālidāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       himavantassa avidūre romaso nāma pabbato  
 tamhi pabbatapādamhi samaṇo bhāvitindriyo  
  
       biḷālike  gahetvāna samaṇassa adāsahaṃ  
 anumodi mahāvīro sayambhu aparājito  
  
       biḷāli te mamaṃ  dinnā vippasannena cetasā  
 bhave nibbattamānemhi phalaṃ nibbattataṃ tava  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ biḷālimadāsahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi biḷāliyā idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā biḷālidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  biḷālidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
    biḷāliyo  machasaṃ    mama  machasaṃ  padipadāyakattherāapadānaṃ  machasaṃ   apaṇṇadipāyattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      macchadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       candabhāgānaditire ukkuso āsahaṃ tadā  
 mahantaṃ macchaṃ paggayha siddhatthamuno adaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ macchamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi macchadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā macchadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  macchadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
      javahaṃsakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vandabhāgānaditire āsiṃ vanacaro tadā  
 siddhatthamadadasaṃ buddhaṃ gacchantamanilañajase  
  
       añajalimpaggahetvāna ullokento mahāmuniṃ  
 sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā avandiṃ nāyakaṃ ahaṃ  
  
              
  
       catunavute ito kappe yamavandiṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā javahaṃsako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  javahaṃsakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      salalapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       candabhāgānaditire ahosiṃ kintaro tadā  
 vipassimaddasaṃ buddhaṃ raṃsijālasamākulaṃ  
  
       pasannacitto sumano paramāya ca pitāyā  
 paggayha salalaṃ pupphaṃ vipassiṃ okiriṃ ahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyiṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā salalapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sallapuppiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
               
  
      upāgatāsayattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       himavantassa vemajjhe saro āsi sunimmito  
 tatthāhaṃ rakkhaso āsiṃ heṭhasilo bhayānako  
  
       anukampako kāruṇiko vipassi lokanāyako  
 mamuddharitukāmo so āgacchi mama santike  
  
       upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 āsayā abhinikkhamma avandiṃ santhuno ahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ vandiṃ purisuttamaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upāgatāsayo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  upāgatāsayattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
              
  
      taraṇiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇo sambuddho vipassi dakkhiṇārabho  
 naditire ṭhito satthā bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato  
  
       nāvā na vijjate tattha santāraṇi mahaṇṇave  
 nadiyā abhinikkhamma tāresiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ tāresiṃ naruttamaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi taraṇāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā taraṇiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  taraṇiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 ukkhepi tela candi ca dīpado ca biḷālido 
 maccho javo salalado rakkhaso taraṇo dasa 
 gāthāyo cettha saṅkhātā tāḷisaṃ cekameva ca  
  ākāsukkhipiyavaggo sattavisatimo   
  
    sattakaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      suvaṇṇabimbohaniyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ekāsanaṃ ahamadaṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
 bimbohanañca pādāsiṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā  
  
       catunavute ito kappe bimbohatamadāsahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bimbohanassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito tesaṭṭhime kappe asamo nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā suvaṇṇabimbohaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  suvaṇṇabimbohaniyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
              
  
      tilamuṭṭhidāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       mama saṃkappamaññāya satthā lokagganāyako  
 mānomayena kāyena iddhiyā upasaṅkami  
  
       satthāramupasaṅkantaṃ vanditvā purisuttamaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano tilamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tilamuṭṭhyā  idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito soḷasakappamhi nandiyo  nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tilamuṭṭhidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tilamuṭṭhidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      caṅgoṭakiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       mahāsamuddaṃ nissāya vasate pabbatantare  
 paccuggantvāna katvāna caṅgoṭakamadāsahaṃ  
  
       siddhatthassa mahesino sabbasattānukampino  
 pupphacaṅgoṭakaṃ datvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ  
  
    tilamuṭṭhiyidaṃ  machasaṃ    tandiso  machasaṃ khattiyo syā  caṅkoṭakiyattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       catunavute ito kappe caṅgoṭakamadaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi caṅgoṭakassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā caṅgoṭakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  caṅgoṭakiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
              
  
      abahañajanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       koṇḍaññassa bhagavato vitarāgassa tādino  
 ākāsasamacittassa  nippapañcassa jhāyino  
  
       sabbamohātivattassa sabbalokahitesino  
 abbhañajanaṃ mayā dinnaṃ dipadindassa satthuno  
  
       aparimeyye ito kappe abbhañajanamadaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi abbhañajanassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito paṇṇarase kappe cirappo nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā abbhañajanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  abbhañajanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      ekañajaliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       udumbare vasantassa niyate paṇṇasanthare  
 vutthekāso mayā dinano samaṇassa mahesino  
  
       tissassa dipadindassa lokanāthassa tādino  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna santhariṃ pupphasanthariṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ kariṃ pupphasantharaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi santharissa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    akakkasacittassa  aṭṭha 
  
               
  
       ito cuddasakappambhi ahosiṃ manujādhipo  
 etañajaliko nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekañajiliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ekañajaliyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
              
  
      potthadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       satthāraṃ dhammamārabbha saṅghañcāpi mahesinaṃ  
 potthadānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ dakkhiṇeyye anuttare  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi potthadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā potthadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  potthadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
      citakapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       candabhāgānaditire anusotaṃ vajāmahaṃ  
 satta māluvapupphāni citamāropayiṃ  ahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe citakaṃ yaṃ apūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi citapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattasaṭṭhimbhito kappe paṭijaggasanāmakā  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  citakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
    mahesino  sīmu    citakamāropayiṃ  simu    citakapujāyidaṃ  simu  
  
               
  
      āluvadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
       pabbate himavattambhi mahāsindhu sudassanā  
 tatthaddasaṃ vitarāgaṃ sappapabhāsaṃ sudassataṃ  
  
       parāmopasame yuttaṃ disvā vimbhitamānaso  
 āluvaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       ekaṃtise ito kappe yamāluvamadaṃ  tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āluvassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āluvadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  āluvadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
              
  
      ekapuṇḍarikattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       romaso nāma nāmena sayambhu subbato  tadā  
 puṇḍarikaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ puṇḍarikamadaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi puṇḍarikassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapuṇḍarīko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ekapuṇḍarikattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      taraṇiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       mahāpathambhi visame setu kārāpito mayā  
 taraṇātthāya lokassa pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       catunavute ito kappe setu kārāpito mayā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       pañcapaññāsito kappe eko āsiṃ samogadho  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā taraṇiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  taraṇiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
    phalamadadiṃ  machasaṃ    sappabho  syā 
  
               
  
 uddānaṃ  
 suvaṇṇaṃ tilamuṭṭhi ca caṅgoṭabbhañaja añajali 
 potthako cita māluvo ekapuṇḍari setunā 
 dvettāḷisagāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi  
  suvaṇṇabimbohanavaggo aṭṭhavisatimo   
  
              
  
      paṇaṇadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       paṇṇasāle nisinnomhi paṇṇabhojanabhojano  
 upaviṭṭhañca maṃ santaṃ upāgacchi mahāmuni  
  
       siddhattho lokapajjoto sabbalokatikicchako  
 tassa paṇṇaṃ mayā dinnaṃ nisinnaṃ  paṇṇasanthare  
  
       catunavute ito  kappe yaṃ paṇṇamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi paṇṇadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paṇṇadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  paṇṇadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
      phaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       sinerusamasantoso dharaṇidharasādiso  
 vuṭṭhihitvā samādimhā bhikkhāya mamupaṭṭhito  
  
       haritakaṃ āmalakaṃ amba jambu vibhiṭakaṃ  
 kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ khillaṃ phārūsakaphalāni ca  
  
       siddhatthassa mahesissa sabbalokānukampino  
 tañca sabbaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattapaññāsito kappe ekajjho nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā phaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
 paladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
  ekāsadamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ  machasaṃ    mahāisi  machasaṃ    nisinnassa  syā    catunna vutino  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
  
      paccuggamaniyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       sihaṃ yathā vanacaraṃ nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā  
 kakudhaṃ vilasantaṃva āgacchantaṃ nanarāsabhaṃ  
  
       siddhatthaṃ lokapajjehaṃ sabbalokatikicchakaṃ  
 akāsiṃ paccuggamanaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe paccuggacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi paccuggamane idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattavise ito kappe eko āsiṃ janādhipo  
 saparivāroti nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paccuggamaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  paccuggamaniyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      ekapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       dakkhiṇambhi duvāramhi pisāvo āsahaṃ tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ pitaraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ  
  
       vipasasissa naraggassa sabbalokahitesino  
 ekapupphaṃ mayā dinnaṃ dipadindassa tādino  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ekapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
               
  
      maghavapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       nammadānadiyā tīre sayambhu aparājito  
 samādhiṃ so samāpanno vippasanno anāvilo  
  
       disvā pasanno sumano sambuddhaṃ aparājitaṃ  
 tāhaṃ maghavapupphena sayambhuṃ pujayiṃ tadā  
  
              
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maghavapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  maghavapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamayaṃ   
  
      upaṭṭhākadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
 dipadindaṃ mahānāgaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       pakkosāpiya tassāhaṃ sabbalokahitesino  
 upaṭṭhāko mayā dinno siddhathessa mahesino  
  
       paṭiggahetvā sambabuddho niyyātesi mahāmuni  
 uṭṭhāya āsanā tamhā pakkāmi pācināmukho  
  
       catunavute ito kappe upaṭṭhākamadaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattapaññāsito kappe balasena sanāmako  
 sattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upaṭṭhākadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  upaṭṭhākadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
               
  
      apadāniyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       apadānaṃ sugatānaṃ kittayiṃhaṃ mahesino  
 pāde ca sirasā vandiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe apadānaṃ pakittayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā apadāniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  apadāniyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamayaṃ   
  
              
  
      sattāhapabbajitattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipassissa bhagavato saṅgho sakkatamānito  
 vyasanaṃ me anuppatataṃ ñātibhedo pure ahu  
  
       pabbajja mubagantvāna vyasanupasamāyahaṃ  
 sattāhābhirato tattha satthusāsanakamyatā  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yamahaṃ pabbajiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pabbajjāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattasaṭṭimbhito kappe satta āsuṃ mahipati  
 sunikkhamāti ñāyanti cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattāhapabbajito thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sattāhapabbajitattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
      buddhupaṭṭhākattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       veṭambariti  me nāmaṃ pitusantaṃ mamaṃ tadā  
 mama hatthaṃ gahetvāna upānayi mahāmuniṃ  
  
       ime maṃ uddisissanti buddhā lokagganāyakā  
 tehaṃ upaṭṭhiṃ sakkaccaṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
  
    voṭambhiniti machasaṃ vedhambhiniti  syā 
  
               
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe buddhe paricariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       tevisambhi ito kappe caturo āsu khattiyo  
 samaṇupaṭṭhākā  nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhupaṭṭhāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
 buddhapaṭṭhākattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
              
  
      pubbaṅgamiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       cullāsitisahassāni pabbajimha akiñcanā  
 tesaṃ pubbaṅgamo āsiṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā  
  
       sarāgā sabhavā  cete vippasnanamanāvilā   
 upaṭṭhahiṃsu sakkaccaṃ pasannā sehi pāṇiha  
  
       khiṇāsavā vantadosā katakiccā anāsavā  
 phariṃsu  mettacittena sayambhu aparājitā  
  
       tesaṃ upaṭṭhahitvāna sambuddhānaṃ patissato  
 maraṇañca anuppatto devattañca agamhase  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yā silamanupālayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saññamassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pubbaṅgamiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pubbaṅgamiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 paṇṇaṃ phalaṃ puccuggamaṃ  ekapupphi ca maghavā 
 upaṭṭhākā padānañca pabbajjā baddhupaṭṭhāko 
 pubbaṅgamo ca gāthāyo aṭṭatāḷisa kitatitāni  
  paṇṇādāyakavaggo ekunatiṃsatimo   
  
    samaṇupaṭṭhakā si mu    samohā  syā    vippasannamanāvilaṃ  simu    pharisuṃ simu    uggamiya  simu 
  
               
  
      citakapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ajito nāma nāmena ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadā  
 āhutiṃ siṭṭhukāmāhaṃ nānāpuphaṃsamānayiṃ  
  
       jalantaṃ citakaṃ disvā sikhino lokabandhuno  
 taṃ ca pupphaṃ samānetvā citake okiriṃ ahaṃ  
  
              
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi budadhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattavise ito kappe sattāsuṃ manujādhipā  
 supajjalitatāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  citakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
      pupphadhārakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vākatiradharo āsiṃ ajānuttaravāsano  
 abhāññāpañcanibbattā candassa parimajjako  
  
       vipassiṃ lokapajjotaṃ disvā ahigataṃ mama  
 pāricchattakapupphāni dhāresiṃ satthuno ahaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhādhārayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhāraṇāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattāsitimbhito kappe eko āsiṃ mahipati  
 samantadhāraṇo nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphadhārako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pupphadhārakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
               
  
      chattadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       putto mama pabbajito kāsāyavasano tadā  
 so ca buddhattaṃ sampatto nibbuto lokapujato  
  
       vicinanto sakaṃ puttaṃ agamaṃ pacchato ahaṃ  
 nibbutassa mahantassa citataṃ agamāsahaṃ  
  
       paggayha añjaliṃ tattha vanditvā citakaṃ ahaṃ  
 setacchattañca paggayha āropesiṃ ahaṃ tadā  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ chattamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi chattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       pañcavise ito kappe satta āsuṃ janādhipā  
 mahāraha sanāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā chattadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  chattadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      saddasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       anuggatamhi ādicce panādo vipulo ahu  
 buddhaseṭṭhassa lokamhi pātubhāvo mahesino  
  
       sadadmassohaṃ tattha na ca passāmi taṃ jinaṃ  
 maraṇe ca anuppatte buddhasaññamanussariṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saddasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  saddasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
               
  
      gosisanikkhepakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ārāmadvārā nikkhamma gosisaṃ santhataṃ mayā  
 anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ājāniyā vātajavā sindhavā sīghavāhanā  
 anubhomi sabbametaṃ gosisassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       aho kāraṃ paramakāraṃ sukhette sukataṃ mayā  
 saṅghe katassa kārassana aññaṃ kalamagghati  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ sisaṃ santhariṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi santharassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       pañcasattatikappamhi suppatiṭṭhita nāmako  
 eko āsiṃ mahātejo cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gosisanikkhepako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  gosisanikkhepakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
              
  
      pādapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       pabbate himavantamhi ahosiṃ kinnaro tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ pitaraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ  
  
       upetaṃ kamahaṃ  buddhaṃ vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 candanaṃ tagarañcāpi pāde osiñcahaṃ tadā  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pādamabhipujayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pādapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pādapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pādapujakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
    upetopi tadā  syā 
  
               
  
      desakittakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       upasāḷhaka nāmohaṃ ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadā  
 kānanaṃ vanamogāḷhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       disvāna vandiṃ pādesu lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ  
 pasannacittaṃ mā ñatvā buddho antaradhāyatha  
  
       kānanā abhinikkhamma buddhaseṭṭhamanussariṃ  
 taṃ desaṃ kittayitvāna kappaṃ saggambhi modahaṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ desamabhikittayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā desakittako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  desakittakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      saraṇagamanayatherāpadānaṃ  
  
       pabbate himavantamhi ahosiṃ luddako ahaṃ  
 vipassiṃ addasaṃ buddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       upāsitvāna sambuddhaṃ veyyāvaccamakāsahaṃ  
 saraṇañca upāgacchiṃ dipadindassa tādino  
  
              
  
       catunavute ito kappe saraṇaṃ yamagacchahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saraṇagamanapphalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saraṇagamaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  saraṇagamaniyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
      ambapiṇḍiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       romaso nāma nāmena dānavo iti vissuto  
 ambabapiṇḍī mayā dinnā  vipassissa mahesino  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yammabamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ambadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
    ambapiṇḍo mayā dinno  syā 
  
               
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambapiṇḍiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ambapiṇḍiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      anusaṃsāvakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       piṇḍāya caramānāhaṃ vipassiṃ addasaṃ jānaṃ  
 uḷuṅkabhikkhaṃ pādāsiṃ dipadindassa tādino  
  
       pasannacitto sumano abhivādesahaṃ tadā  
 anusaṃsāvayiṃ buddhaṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā  
  
       catunavute ito kappe anusaṃsāvayiṃ ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi anusaṃsāvanāphalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anusaṃsāvako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  anusaṃsāvakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 citakaṃ pārichatto ca sadda gosisasantharaṃ 
 padaṃ padesaṃ saraṇaṃ ambo saṃsāvako pi ca 
 sattāḷisa gāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi  
  citakapujakavaggo tiṃsatimo  
  
              
  
 atha vagguddānaṃ  
 kaṇikāro hatthidado ālambaṇudakāsanaṃ 
 tuvaraṃ thomako veca ukkhepaṃ sisupadhānaṃ 
 paṇṇado citapuji ca gāthāyo ceva sabbaso 
 cattāri ca satāniha ekapaññāsameva ca  
 pañcavisasatā sabbā dvāsattati taduttari  
 tisataṃ apadānānaṃ gaṇitā atthadassihi  
  tatiyaṃ satakaṃ  samattaṃ  
    kaṇikāravaggadasakaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      padumakesariyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       isisaṅghe ahaṃ pubbe āsiṃ mātaṅgavāraṇo  
 mahesinaṃ pasādena padamakesaramokiriṃ 
  
       paccekajinaseṭṭhesu dhutarāgesu tādisu  
 tesu cittaṃ pasādetvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe kesaraṃ okiriṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumakesariyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
 padumakesariyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
      sabbagandhiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       gandhamālaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vipassissa mahesino  
 adāsiṃ ujubhūtassa koseyyaṃ vatthamuttamaṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ gandhamadadiṃ  pure  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi gandhadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       ito paṇṇarase kappe sucelo nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbagandhiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sabbagandhiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      paramannadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ udayantaṃva bhānumaṃ  
 vipassimaddasaṃ buddhaṃ lokejeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       añajalimpaggahetvāna abhinesiṃ  sakaṃ gharaṃ  
 abhinetvāna  sambuddhaṃ paramannaṃ adāsahaṃ  
  
    vatthamadadiṃ  simu    atinesiṃ  sīmu    atinetvāna  simu 
  
               
  
       ekanavute ito kappe paramannaṃ dadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi paramannasisidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paramannadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  paramannadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      dhammasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vipassino bhagavato mahābodhimaho ahu  
 rukkhaṭṭhe yeva  sambuddhe lokajeṭṭhe narāsabhe  
  
       bhagavā tamhi samaye bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato  
 catusaccaṃ pakāseti vācāsabhimudirayaṃ  
  
       saṅkhittena ca desenno vitthārena ca desayaṃ   
 vivaṭṭacchado sambuddho nibbāpesi mahājanaṃ  
  
       tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 vanditvā satthuno pāde pakkāmi uttarāmukho  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ dhammamasuniṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhammasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ    
  
       tettiṃsamhi ito kappe eko āsiṃ mahipati  
 sutavā nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhammasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  dhammasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
              
  
      phalasāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       bhāgirathinaditire ahosi assamo tadā  
 tamahaṃ assamaṃ gacchiṃ phalahattho apekkhavā   
  
       vipassiṃ tattha addakkhiṃ pitaraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ  
 yaṃ me atthi phalaṃ sabbaṃ adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ 
  
    rukkhaṭṭhasseva smabuddho  machasaṃ    desiyi  syā    dhamamasavassidaṃ phalaṃ  machasaṃ dhammasavaṇassidaṃphalaṃ  simu    apekhavā  simu 
  
               
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā phaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  phaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
      sampasādakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       namo te buddhaviratthu vippamuttosi sabbadhi  
 vyasanaṃ hi  anuppatto tassa me saraṇaṃ bhava  
  
       siddhattho tassa vyākāsi loke appaṭipuggalo  
 mahodadhisamo saṅgho appameyyo anuttaro  
  
       tattha tvaṃ viraje khette anantaphaladāyake  
 saṅgho cittaṃ pasādehi  subījaṃ vāpi  ropaya  
  
       idaṃ vavona sabbaññu lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 mamevaṃ  anusāsitvā vehāsaṃ nabhamuggami  
  
       aciraṃ gatamattamhi sabbaññumhi narāsabhe  
 maraṇaṃ samanuppatto tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
       tadāhaṃ viraje khette anantaphaladāyake  
 saṅghe cittaṃ pasadetvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito  kappe pasādamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pasādassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sampasādāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sampasādakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
    byasanamhi  machasaṃ    pasādetvā  masaṃ    cāpa  machasaṃ    mameva  machasaṃ    catunnavutito  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
  
      ārāmadākattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato ārāmo ropito mayā  
 sandacchāyesu rukkhesu upasantesu pakkhisu  
  
       addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
 ārāmaṃ atināmesiṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena phalaṃ pupphañcadāsahaṃ   
 tato jātappasādo ca  taṃ vanaṃ pariṇāmayiṃ  
  
       buddhassa yamidaṃ dāsiṃ vippasannena cetasā  
 bhave nibbattamānamhi nibbattati phalaṃ mama  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yamārāmaṃ phalaṃ dadiṃ  tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ārāmassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattatiṃse ito kappe sattāsuṃ mudusitalā  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ārāmadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ārāmadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      anulepadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       atthadassa munino addasaṃ sāvakaṃ ahaṃ  
 kavakammaṃ karontassa simāya upagacchahaṃ  
  
       niṭṭhite kavakamme ca anulepamadāsahaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano puññakkhette anuttare 
  
       aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi anulepassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anulepadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  anulepadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    phalaṃ pupphamadāsahaṃ  machasaṃ    padādo ca  simu    yaṃ ārāmamadaṃ tadā  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
  
      buddhasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       udentaṃ sataraṃsiṃva pitarāsiṃva bhānumaṃ  
 vanantaragataṃ santaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
       addasaṃ supinattena siddhatthaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā sugatiṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  buddhasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      pabahāradāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       piyadassino bhagavato pabhāro sodhito mayā  
 ghaṭakañca upaṭṭhāsiṃ paribhogāya tādino  
  
       taṃ me buddho viyākāsi piyadassi mahāmuni  
 sahassakaṇḍo satabheṇḍu dhajālu haritāmayo  
  
       nibbattissati so yupo ratanañca anappakaṃ  
 pabbhāradānaṃ datvāna kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ  
  
       ito khattiṃsakappamhi susuddho nāma khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pabbhāradāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pabbhāradāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddanaṃ  
 kesaraṃ gandha mannañca dhammasaññi elena ca  
 pasādārāmadāyī ca lepako buddhasaññako  
 pabbhārado ca gāthāyo ekapaññāsa kittiyā  
  padumakesariyavaggo  ekatiṃsatimo   
  
               
              
  
      ārakkhadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       dhammadassassa munino vati kārāpitā mayā  
 ārakkho ca mayā dinno dipadindassa  tādino  
  
       aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā  
 tena kammavisesena patto me āsavakkhayo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ārakkhadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ārakkhadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
      bhojanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       sujāto sālalaṭṭhiva sobhañajanamivuggato  
 indalaṭṭhirivākāse virocati sadā jino  
  
       tassa devātidevassa vessabhussa mahesino  
 adāsiṃ bhojanamahaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
  
       taṃ me buddho anumodi sayambhu aparājito  
 bhave nibbattamānambhi phalaṃ nibbattatu tava 
  
       ekatiṃse  ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhojanassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       pañcavise ito kappe eko āsiṃ amittabho   
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhojanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  bhojanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      gatasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       ākāse ca  natthi ambare anilañajase  
 siddhatheṃ jinamadadakkhiṃ gacchantaṃ ticivaṅgaṇe  
  
       anileneritaṃ disvā sammāsambuddhacīvaraṃ  
 vitti me tāvade jātaṃ  disvāna gamanaṃ mune   
  
    davipadindassa  machasaṃ    ekattiṃse  machasaṃ    amittako  machasaṃ    ākāseca  machasaṃ    tidicaṅgaṇaṃ  syā    vitti mamāhu tāvade  machasaṃ    muniṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhi tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gatasaññaka thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  gatasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
      sattapadumiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       nadikule masāmahaṃ nesādo nāma brāhmaṇo  
 satapattehi pupphehi sammajajitvāna assamaṃ  
  
       suvaṇaṃṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ siddhatthaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 disvā vanena  gacchantaṃ hāso me upapajjatha  
  
       paccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 assamaṃ atināmetvā jalajaggehi okiriṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ito tesattame kappe caturo pādapāvarā  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattapadumiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sattapadumiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      pupaphāsanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ sataraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ  
 avidūrena gacchantaṃ siddhatthaṃ aparājitaṃ  
  
       tassa paccuggamitvāna pavesetvāna assamaṃ  
 pupphāsanaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
  
       añajalimpaggahetvāna vedajāto tadā ahaṃ  
 buddhe cittaṃ pasādetvā taṃ kammaṃ pariṇāmayiṃ  
  
              
  
       yaṃ me atthi kataṃ puññaṃ sayambhumhaparājite  
 sabbe tena kusalena vimalo homi sāsane  
  
    nabhena  sīmu  machasaṃ    pitaraṃsiṃva  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       catunavute ito kappe pupphāsanamadaṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphāsanassadaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphāsanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pupphāsanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
      āsanatthavikattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       cetiyaṃ uttamaṃ nāma sikhino lokabandhuno  
 araññe irine  vane andhābhiṇḍāmahaṃ tadā  
  
       pavanā nikkhamitvāna diṭṭhaṃ sihāsanaṃ mayā  
 ekaṃsaṃ añjaliṃ katvā thavissaṃ  lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       divasabhāgaṃ thavitvāna buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena imaṃ vācamudīrayiṃ  
  
       namo te purisājañña namo te purisuttama  
 sabbaññusi mahāvīra lokajeṭṭha narāsabha 
  
       abhitthavitthā sikhinaṃ nimittakaraṇenahaṃ  
 āsanaṃ abhivādetvā pakkāmi uttarāmukho  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe santhaviṃ  vadataṃ varaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thomanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattatiṃse ito kappe atulyā  satta assu te  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āsanatthaviko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  āsanatthavikattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
    irine  machasaṃ    santhaviṃ  machasaṃ    yaṃ thaviṃ  machasaṃ    atulaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
  
      saddasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       sudassano mahāvīro desenno amataṃ padaṃ  
 parivuto sāvakehi vasati gharamuttame  
  
       tāya vācāya madhurāya saṅgaṇhāti  mahājanaṃ  
 ghoso ca vipulo āsi āsaṃso  devamānuse  
  
       nigghosasasaddaṃ sutvāna siddhatthassa mahesino  
 sadde cittaṃ pasadetvā avandiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saddasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  saddasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
      tiraṃsiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kesariṃ abhijātaṃva aggikkhandhaṃ pabbate  
 obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā  siddhatthaṃ pabbatantare  
  
       suriyassa ca ālokaṃ candālokaṃ tatheva ca  
 buddhālokañca disvāna vitti me udapajjatha  
  
       tayo āloke disvāna buddhañca  sāvakuttamaṃ  
 ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
  
       tayo hi ālokakarā loke lokatamonudā  
 cando ca suriyo cāpi buddho ca lokanāyako  
  
       opammamupadassetvā kittino me mahāmuni  
 buddhassa vaṇṇaṃ kittetvā kappaṃ saggamhi mohadahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ buddhamabhikittayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
              
  
       ekasaṭṭhimbhito kappe eko ñāṇadharo ahu  
 sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiraṃsiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  tiraṃsiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    saṅgaṇahante  simu    āsi so  machasaṃ    disāsinnaṃ  syā    upapajjathaṃ  simu    sambudadhaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      kandalipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       sindhuyā nadiyā tīre ahosiṃ kassako tadā  
 parakammāyane yutto parabhattaṃ apassito  
  
       sindhumanucarantohaṃ siddhatthaṃ jinamaddasaṃ  
 samādhinā nisinnaṃva satapattaṃva puppitaṃ  
  
       satta kandalipupphāni vaṇṭe chetvānahaṃ tadā  
 matthake abhiropesiṃ buddhassādiccabandhuno  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ anukūle samāhitaṃ  
 tidhā pahinnamātaṅgaṃ kuñajaraṃva durāsadaṃ  
  
       tamahaṃ upagantvāna nipakaṃ bhāvitindriyaṃ  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna avandiṃ satthuno ahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kandalipphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  kandalipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ kavamaṃ   
  
      kumudamāliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       usabhaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ mahesiṃ vijitāvinaṃ  
 vipassinaṃ mahāvīraṃ abhijātaṃva kesariṃ  
  
       rathiyaṃ paṭijjantaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ  
 gahetvā kumudaṃ mālaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ samokiriṃ  
  
              
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kumudamāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  kumudamāliyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 ārakkhado bhojananado gatasaññi padumiyo  
 pupphāsani santhaviko saddasaññī tiraṃsiko 
 kandaliko kumudī ca sattapaññāsa gāthakā  
  ārakkhadāyakavaggo khatatiṃsatimo   
  
               
  
      ummāpupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       samāhitaṃ samāpannaṃ siddhatthamaparājitaṃ  
 samādhinā upaviṭṭhaṃ addasāhaṃ naruttamaṃ  
  
       ummāpupphaṃ gahetvāna buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
 sabbe pupphā ekasīsā uddhavaṇṭā  adhomukhā  
  
       sucittā viya tiṭṭhanne ākāse pupphasanthare   
 tena cittappasādena tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito  kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       pañcapaññāsiko kappe eko āsiṃ mahipati  
 samantacchadano nāma cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ummāpupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  ummāpupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
              
  
      pulitapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kakudhaṃ vipasantaṃva nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā  
 osadhiṃva virocantaṃ obhāsantaṃ nārāsabhaṃ  
  
       añjaliṃ paggahetvāna avandiṃ santhuno ahaṃ  
 satthāraṃ parivaṇṇesiṃ sakakammena tosito  
  
       susuddhaṃ pulitaṃ gayha gatamagge samokiriṃ  
 ucchaṅgena gahetvāna vipassissa mahesino  
  
       tato upaḍḍhapulinaṃ vippasannena cetasā  
 divāvihāre osiñciṃ dipadindassa tādino  
  
       catunavute ito kappe pulinaṃ yamasiñcahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pulinassa idaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pulinapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pulinapujakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
  umāpupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  machasaṃ    udadhaṃvaṇṭā  machasaṃ    pupphasantharā  machasaṃ    catunnavutito  machasaṃ    tosayiṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
      hāsajanakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       dumagge paṃsukūlakaṃ  laggaṃ satthuno  
 añajalimpaggahetvāna bhiyyo uccaritaṃ mayā  
  
       durato patidissāna  haso me udapajjatha   
 añajalimpaggahetvāna bhiyyo cittaṃ padādayiṃ  
  
       ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā hāsajanako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  hāsajanakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
              
  
      yaññasāmikattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       jātiyā satatvassohaṃ ahosiṃ mantapāragu  
 kulavaṃsaṃ  adhāresiṃ yañño usasāhito mayā  
  
       cullāsitisahassāni pasu haññanti me tadā  
 sārathambhupanitāni  yaññatthāya upaṭṭhitā  
  
       ukkāmukhapahaṭṭhova khadiraṅgārasannibho  
 udayantova suriyo puṇṇamāseva candimā  
  
       siddhattho sabbasiddhattho tilokambhito hito  
 upagantvāna sambuddho idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
       ahiṃsā sabbapāṇānaṃ kumāra mama ruccati  
 theyyā ca aticārā ca majjapānā ca ārati  
  
       rati ca samacariyāya bāhusaccaṃ kataññutā  
 diṭṭhe dhamme parattha ca ete dhammā pasaṃsiyā  
  
       ete dhamme bhāvayitvā sabbasattahite rato  
 buddhe citataṃ pasādetvā bhāvehi maggamuttamaṃ 
  
       idaṃ vatvāna sabbaññu lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 mamevamanusāsitvā vehāsamuggato gato 
  
       pubbe cittaṃ visedhetvā pacchā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 tena cittappasādena tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
  
    paṃsukulikaṃ  syā    pana disvāna  machasaṃ    upapajjatha  simu    kulavattaṃ  machasaṃ    sārasamiṃ  hi upatitāni  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       catunavute ito kappe yadā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā yaññasāmiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  yaññasāmikattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
              
  
      nimittasaññakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vandahāgānaditire vasāmi assame ahaṃ  
 suvaṇṇamiga maddakkhiṃ carantaṃ vipite ahaṃ  
  
       mige citteṃ pasādetvā lokajeṭṭamanussariṃ  
 tena cittappasādena aññe buddhe anussariṃ  
  
       abbhatitā ca ye buddhā vattamānā anāgatā  
 evameva virocanti migarājāva te tayo  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       sattavise ito kappe eko āsiṃ mahipati  
 araññasatto nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nimittasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  nimittasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
      annasaṃsāvakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe  
 kañcanagaghiyasaṅkāsaṃ khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ  
  
       siddhatthaṃ sabbasiddhatthaṃ anejamaparājitaṃ  
 sambuddhaṃ atināmetvā bhojayiṃ taṃ mahāmuni  
  
       muni kāruṇiko loke obhāsayi mamaṃ tadā  
 buddhe cittaṃ pasādetvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ  
  
               
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ananasaṃsāvako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  annasaṃsāvayakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
              
  
      nigguṇḍipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       yadā devo devakāyā cavati āyusaṅkhayā  
 tayo saddā niccharanti devānaṃ anumodataṃ  
  
       ito bho sugatiṃ gaccha manussānaṃ sahavyataṃ  
 manussabhuto saddhamme labha saddhamanuttaraṃ  
  
       sā te saddhā niviṭṭhassa mulajātā patiṭṭhitā  
 yāvajīvaṃ asaṃhirā saddhamme suppavedite  
  
       kāyena kusalaṃ katvā vācāya kusalaṃ bahu  
 manasā kusalaṃ katvā abyāpajjaṃ nirūpadhiṃ  
  
       tato opadhikaṃ puññaṃ katvā dānena taṃ bahuṃ  
 aññepi macce saddhamme brahmacariye nivesaya 
  
       imāya anukampāya devā devaṃ yadā viduṃ  
 cavantaṃ ṃanumodanti ehi devapuraṃ puna 
  
       imāya anukampāya devā devaṃ yadā viduṃ  
 cavantaṃ anumodanti ehi devapuraṃ puna 
  
       mama saṃvegamaññāya samaṇo bhāvitinduyo  
 mamuddharitukāmo so āgacchi mama santike  
  
       sumano nāma nāmena padumuttarasāvako  
 atthadhammānusāsitvā saṃvejesi mamaṃ tadā  
  dvādasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ    
  
       tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā buddhe cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 taṃ ciramabhivādetvā  tattha kālakato ahaṃ  
  
    saṃviggohaṃ  machasaṃ    kaṃ su  machasaṃ    dhiraṃ abivādetvā machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       upapajjisaṃ  tattheva sukkamūlena codito  
 vasanto mātukucchimbhi puna dhārisa  mātuyā  
  
       tamhā kāyā cavitvāna tidase upapajjahaṃ  
 etthantare na passāmi domanassamahaṃ tadā  
  
              
  
       tāvatiṃsā cavitvāna mātukucchiṃ samokkamiṃ  
 nikkhamitvāna kucchimhā kaṇhasukkamajānahaṃ  
  
       jātiyā sattavassova  ārāmaṃ pāvisiṃ ahaṃ  
 gotamassa bhagavato sakyaputtassa tādino  
  
       vitthārite  pāvacane bāhujaññamhi sāsane  
 addasaṃ sāsanakare bhikkhavo tattha santhuno  
  
       sāvatthi nāma nagaraṃ rājā tatthāsi kosalo  
 rathena nāgayuttena upesi bodhimuttamaṃ  
  
       tassāhaṃ nāgaṃ disvāna pubbakammamanussariṃ  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna samayaṃ agamāsabhaṃ  
  
       jātiyā sattavasseva pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
 yo so buddhaṃ upaṭṭhāsi ānando nāma sāvako  
  
       gatimā dhitimā ceva satimā ca bahussuto  
 rañño cittaṃ pasādento niyyādesi mahājuti  
  
       tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna pubbakammamanussariṃ  
 tattheva ṭhitako santo arahattamapāpuṇiṃ  
  
       ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā sire katvāna añjaliṃ  
 sambuddhamabhivādetvā imaṃ vācamudirayiṃ  
  
       padumuttarabuddhassa dipadindassa  santhuno  
 nigguṇḍipupphaṃ paggayha sihāsane ṭhapesahaṃ  
  
       tena kammena dipadinda lokaṭṭhe narāsabha  
 pattombhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
    upapajjiṃ  machasaṃ upapajjissaṃ  si sabbattha    dhāreti  sabbattha dhārisaṃkammatthavasena gahetabbaṃ     jātiyā sattavassena  syā    vithorike  machasaṃ    dvipadindassa  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       pañcavisasahassamhi kappānaṃ manujādhipā  
 abbudanirabbudāni aṭṭhaṭṭhāsiṃsu khattiyā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nigguṇḍipupphayo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  nigguṇaḍipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattaṃ   
  
              
  
      sumanāveliyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       vessabhussa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino    
 sabbe janā samāgamma mahāpujaṃ karonti te  
  
       sudhāya piṇḍaṃ katvāna āvelaṃ sumanāyahaṃ  
 sihāsanassa purato abhiropesahaṃ tadā  
  
       sabbe janā samāgamama pekkhanti pupphamuttamaṃ  
 kenidaṃ pujitaṃ pupphaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino  
  
       tena cittappasādena nimmāṇaṃ upapajjahaṃ  
 anubhosiṃ  sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatamattano  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 sabbesānaṃ piyo homi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
       nābhijānāmi kāyena vācāya uda cetasā  
 saṃyatānaṃ tapassinaṃ kataṃ akkositaṃ mayā  
  
       tena sucaritenāhaṃ cittassa paṇidhihi ca  
 sabbesaṃ pujino homi anakkossidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyiidaṃ phalaṃ   
  
       ito ekādase kappe sahassārosi khattiyo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavattī mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumanāveliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  sumanāveliyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    anubhomi  machasaṃ    esā gāthā machasaṃ potthake natthi 
  
               
  
      pupaphachattiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 saccaṃ pakāsayantassa nibbāpentassa pāṇito  
  
       jalajaṃ āharitvāna satapattaṃ manoramaṃ  
 pupphassa chattaṃ katvāna buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
              
  
       siddhattho ca lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggabho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satho imaṃ gāthaṃ  abhāsatha  
  
       yo me cittaṃ pasādetvā pupphachattaṃ adhārayi  
 tena cittappasādena duggatiṃ so na gacchati 
  
       idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho siddhattho lokanāyako  
 uyyojetvāna parisaṃ vehāsaṃ nabhamuggami  
  
       vuṭṭhite naradevambhi setacchattampi vuṭṭhahi  
 purato buddhaseṭṭhassa gacchati chattamuttamaṃ  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ chattamabhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphachattassidaṃ phalaṃ   
  
       catusatatatikappamhi aṭṭha jalayikhā ahu  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavattī mahabbalo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphachattiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  pupphachattiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      saparivārachattadāyakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho  
 akāse jalavuṭṭhiva vassati dhammavuṭṭhiyā  
  
       tamadadasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ  
 sakaṃ cittaṃ padādetvā agamāsiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ  
  
       chattaṃ alaṅkataṃ gayha upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ  
  
       susaṅgahitayāvaṃva dāntova sācakuttamo  
 upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ matthake sampatiṭṭhahi  
  
       anukampako kāruṇiko buddho lokagganāyako  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha  
  
    imā gāthā sīmu    ādhārayiṃ  machasaṃ akārayi  sīmu 
  
               
  
       yena chattamidaṃ dinnaṃ alaṅkataṃ manoramaṃ  
 tena cittappasādena duggatiṃ so na gacchati  
  
              
  
       sattakkhattuñca devesu devarajjaṃ karissati  
 khattiṃsakkhattuṃ rājā ca  cakkavatti bhavissati  
  
       kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhāvo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati  
  
       tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
       buddhassa giramaññāya vācāsabhimudiritaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano bhiyyo hāsaṃ janesahaṃ  
  
       jahitvā mānusiṃ yoniṃ devayoniṃ  samajjhagaṃ  
 vimānamuttamaṃ mayhaṃ abbhuggataṃ manoramaṃ  
  
       vimānā nikkhamantassa detacchattaṃ dharīyati  
 tadā saññaṃ paṭilabhiṃ pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       devalokā cavitvāna manussatattañca āgamiṃ  
 chattiṃsakkhattuṃ cakkavatti sattakappasatambhito 
  
       tamhā kāyā cavitvāna āgañachiṃ tidasaṃ puraṃ  
 saṃsaritvā nupubbena mānussaṃ punarāgamiṃ  
  
       okkāntaṃ mātukucchiṃ maṃ setacchattamadhārayuṃ  
 jātiyā sattavassohaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
  
       sunando nāma nāmena brāhmaṇo mantapāragu  
 phalikaṃ chattamādāya sāvakaggassa so adā  
  
       anumodi mahāvīro sāriputto mahākathi  
 sutvānumodanaṃ tassa pubbakammamanussariṃ  
  
       añajalimpaggahetvāna sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 saritvā purimaṃ kammaṃ arahattamapāpuṇaṃ  
  
       uṭṭhāya āsanā tamhā sire katvāna añjaliṃ  
 sambuddhamabhivādetvā imaṃ vācamudirayiṃ  
  
       satasahasse ito kappe buddho loke anuttaro  
 padumuttaro lokavidu ahutinaṃ paṭiggaho  
  
    khattiṃsakkhattuñca rājā  machasaṃ    dibbaṃ yoniṃ  machasaṃ dibbayoniṃ  syā    tadā  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       tassa chattaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vicittaṃ samalaṅkataṃ  
 ubho hatthehi paggaṇhi sayambhu aggapuggalo  
  
              
  
       aho buddho aho dhammo aho no satthu sampadā  
 ekacchattassa dānane duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
       kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saparivārajattadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  saparivārajattadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 uddānaṃ  
 ummāpupphañca pulinaṃ haso yañño nimittako  
 saṃsāvako nigguṇḍi ca sumanaṃ pupphachattako  
 saparivārachatto ca gāthā sattasatuttarā  
  ummāpupphiyavaggo tettiṃsatimo   
  
      gandhadhupiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       siddhatthassa bhagavato gandhadhupamadāsahaṃ  
 sumanehi paṭicchannaṃ buddhānucchavikañca taṃ  
  
       kañcanagaghiyasaṅkā saṃ sambuddhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   
 indivaraṃva jalitaṃ ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ  
  
       vyagghusabhaṃva pavaraṃ abhijātaṃva kesariṃ  
 nisinnaṃ samaṇānaggabhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ 
  
       disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā paggahetvāna añaliṃ  
 vanditvā satthuno pāde pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho  
  
       catunavute ito kappe yaṃ gandhamadadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi gandhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhadhupiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  gandhadhupiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ  machasaṃ

      udakapujakattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ gacchantaṃ anilañajase  
 ghatāsanaṃva jalitaṃ ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ  
  
       pāṇinā udakaṃ gayha ākase ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ  
 sampaṭicci mahāvīro buddho kāruṇiko isi  
  
       antalikkhe ṭhito satthā padumuttaranāmako  
 mama saṅkappamaññāya imaṃ gāthamabhāsatha  
  
       iminā dakadānena pitiupapādenena ca  
 kappasatasahassampi duggatiṃ nupapajjasi  
  
       tena kammena dipadinda lokajeṭṭa narāsabha  
 pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā jayaparājayaṃ  
  
       sahassarājanāmenana tayoca cakkavattino  
 pañcasaṭṭhikappasate cāturantā janādhipā  
  
       paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime  
 chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti  
  udakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
      punnāgapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ  
  
       kānanaṃ vanamogayha vasāmi luddako ahaṃ  
 punnāgaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā buddhaseṭaṭhaṃ anussariṃ  
  
       taṃ pupphaṃ ocinitvāna sugandhaṃ gandhitaṃ subhaṃ  
 thupaṃ karitvā  puline buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  
  
       dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
       ekambhi navute kappe eko āsiṃ tamonudo  
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavattī mahabbalo
